  function toggleDesignArea(id) {
    const card = document.getElementById('design-area-' + id);
    card.classList.toggle('expanded');
  }


  function updateDesignAreaMeta(id) {
    const hazard = document.getElementById('da-hazard-' + id)?.value || '';
    const area = document.getElementById('da-area-' + id)?.value || '';
    const meta = document.getElementById('da-meta-' + id);
    if (!meta) return;
    let parts = [];
    if (hazard) parts.push(hazard.replace(' — ', ' '));
    if (area) parts.push(area + ' sq ft');
    meta.textContent = parts.join('  |  ');
  }


  function removeDesignArea(id) {
    const card = document.getElementById('design-area-' + id);
    if (card) {
      card.style.opacity = '0';
      card.style.transform = 'translateX(-8px)';
      card.style.transition = 'all 0.2s ease';
      setTimeout(() => {
        card.remove();
        // Show empty state if no areas remain
        const list = document.getElementById('design-area-list');
        if (list && list.children.length === 0) showDesignAreaEmpty();
      }, 200);
    }
  }


  function showDesignAreaEmpty() {
    const list = document.getElementById('design-area-list');
    if (!list) return;
    list.innerHTML = `<div class="design-area-empty">
      <div class="design-area-empty-icon">💧</div>
      No design areas added yet. Click <strong>+ Add Design Area</strong> above to begin.
    </div>`;
  }


  // Initialize empty state on load
  function initDesignAreas() {
    const list = document.getElementById('design-area-list');
    if (list) showDesignAreaEmpty();
  }




  // ── SUPPLEMENTS ──
  const SUPPLEMENTS = {
    restaurant:   { label: 'Restaurant / Food Service', icon: '🍳', section: 'supp-restaurant' },
    woodworking:  { label: 'Woodworking / Lumber',      icon: '🪚', section: 'supp-woodworking' },
    warehouse:    { label: 'Warehouse / Distribution',  icon: '🏭', section: 'supp-warehouse' },
    autoservice:  { label: 'Auto Service / Repair',     icon: '🔧', section: 'supp-autoservice' },
    sprinkler:    { label: 'Sprinkler — Detailed',      icon: '💧', section: 'supp-sprinkler' },
    apartments:   { label: 'Apartments / Condominiums', icon: '🏢', section: 'supp-apartments' },
    addbuilding:  { label: 'Additional Buildings',      icon: '🏗️', section: 'supp-addbuilding' },
  };


  // ── GL MODULES ──
  const GL_MODULES = {
    premises: { label: 'Premises Liability', icon: '🏛️', section: 'gl-premises' },
    products: { label: 'Products Liability', icon: '📦', section: 'gl-products' },
    fleet:    { label: 'Small Fleet',        icon: '🚛', section: 'gl-fleet' },
  };


  const activeGL = new Set();


  function toggleGL(id) {
    const card = document.getElementById('gl-card-' + id);
    const label = card.querySelector('.supp-toggle-label');
    const isActive = activeGL.has(id);
    if (isActive) {
      activeGL.delete(id);
      card.classList.remove('active-supp');
      label.textContent = 'Inactive';
      removeGLNav(id);
    } else {
      activeGL.add(id);
      card.classList.add('active-supp');
      label.textContent = 'Active';
      addGLNav(id);
    }
  }


  function addGLNav(id) {
    const container = document.getElementById('gl-nav-items');
    if (document.getElementById('gl-nav-' + id)) return;
    const m = GL_MODULES[id];
    const div = document.createElement('div');
    div.className = 'supp-nav-item';
    div.id = 'gl-nav-' + id;
    div.setAttribute('data-section', m.section);
    div.onclick = function() { showSection(m.section, this); };
    div.innerHTML = '<div class="supp-dot"></div> ' + m.icon + ' ' + m.label + '<span class="supp-badge">GL</span>';
    container.appendChild(div);
  }


  function removeGLNav(id) {
    const el = document.getElementById('gl-nav-' + id);
    if (el) el.remove();
    const active = document.querySelector('.section-panel.active');
    if (active && active.id === 'section-' + GL_MODULES[id].section) {
      showSection('gl-manager', document.querySelector('[data-section="gl-manager"]'));
    }
  }


  // Occupancy → supplement mapping for auto-suggest
  const OCCUPANCY_MAP = {
    'Restaurant / Food Service':  ['restaurant'],
    'Woodworking / Lumber':       ['woodworking'],
    'Warehouse / Distribution':   ['warehouse'],
    'Auto Service / Repair':      ['autoservice'],
    'Apartments / Condominiums':  ['apartments'],
  };


  const activeSupplements = new Set();
  const suggestedSupplements = new Set();


  function handleOccupancyChange(val) {
    // Clear previous suggestions
    suggestedSupplements.forEach(id => {
      const badge = document.getElementById('supp-card-' + id)?.querySelector('.auto-suggested');
      if (badge) badge.remove();
    });
    suggestedSupplements.clear();


    const matches = OCCUPANCY_MAP[val] || [];
    matches.forEach(id => {
      suggestedSupplements.add(id);
      const card = document.getElementById('supp-card-' + id);
      if (card && !card.querySelector('.auto-suggested')) {
        const badge = document.createElement('div');
        badge.className = 'auto-suggested';
        badge.textContent = 'AUTO-SUGGESTED';
        card.appendChild(badge);
      }
      // Auto-activate if not already active
      if (!activeSupplements.has(id)) {
        toggleSupplement(id);
      }
    });


    if (matches.length > 0) {
      // Show a non-blocking notice instead of alert
      showSuppToast(matches.map(id => SUPPLEMENTS[id].label).join(', '));
    }
  }


  function showSuppToast(names) {
    let toast = document.getElementById('supp-toast');
    if (!toast) {
      toast = document.createElement('div');
      toast.id = 'supp-toast';
      toast.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;bottom:80px;left:50%;transform:translateX(-50%);background:#0d1b2a;color:#e2c97e;padding:10px 20px;border-radius:8px;font-size:13px;font-family:IBM Plex Sans,sans-serif;z-index:999;box-shadow:0 4px 20px rgba(0,0,0,0.3);border:1px solid #c9a84c;transition:opacity 0.4s;';
      document.body.appendChild(toast);
    }
    toast.textContent = '✓ Supplement auto-activated: ' + names;
    toast.style.opacity = '1';
    setTimeout(() => { toast.style.opacity = '0'; }, 3500);
  }


  function toggleSupplement(id) {
    const card = document.getElementById('supp-card-' + id);
    const label = card.querySelector('.supp-toggle-label');
    const isActive = activeSupplements.has(id);


    if (isActive) {
      activeSupplements.delete(id);
      card.classList.remove('active-supp');
      label.textContent = 'Inactive';
      removeSuppNav(id);
    } else {
      activeSupplements.add(id);
      card.classList.add('active-supp');
      label.textContent = 'Active';
      addSuppNav(id);
    }
    updateProgress();
  }


  function addSuppNav(id) {
    const container = document.getElementById('supp-nav-items');
    if (document.getElementById('supp-nav-' + id)) return;
    const s = SUPPLEMENTS[id];
    const div = document.createElement('div');
    div.className = 'supp-nav-item';
    div.id = 'supp-nav-' + id;
    div.setAttribute('data-section', s.section);
    div.onclick = function() { showSection(s.section, this); };
    div.innerHTML = '<div class="supp-dot"></div> ' + s.icon + ' ' + s.label + '<span class="supp-badge">SUPP</span>';
    container.appendChild(div);
  }


  function removeSuppNav(id) {
    const el = document.getElementById('supp-nav-' + id);
    if (el) el.remove();
    // If currently viewing this supplement, go back to manager
    const active = document.querySelector('.section-panel.active');
    if (active && active.id === 'section-' + SUPPLEMENTS[id].section) {
      showSection('supp-manager', document.querySelector('[data-section="supp-manager"]'));
    }
  }

        <div class="field form-full" style="margin-top:8px;">
          <label>Protection Notes</label>
          <textarea id="${b}-protection-notes" rows="3" placeholder="Sprinkler coverage details, alarm panel location, deficiencies noted..."></textarea>
        </div>
      </div>


      <div class="divider"></div>


      <!-- E — Exposure -->
      <div style="padding:0 16px 14px;">
        <div style="font-size:10px;font-weight:600;color:var(--navy);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.08em;margin-bottom:10px;padding-top:12px;">E — Exposure</div>
        <div class="form-grid">
          <div class="field">
            <label>Exposure — North</label>
            <input type="text" id="${b}-exposure-north" placeholder="Adjacent occupancy / distance">
          </div>
          <div class="field">
            <label>Exposure — South</label>
            <input type="text" id="${b}-exposure-south" placeholder="Adjacent occupancy / distance">
          </div>
          <div class="field">
            <label>Exposure — East</label>
            <input type="text" id="${b}-exposure-east" placeholder="Adjacent occupancy / distance">
          </div>
          <div class="field">
            <label>Exposure — West</label>
            <input type="text" id="${b}-exposure-west" placeholder="Adjacent occupancy / distance">
          </div>
        </div>
        <div class="field form-full" style="margin-top:8px;">
          <label>Exposure / General Notes</label>
          <textarea id="${b}-exposure-notes" rows="3" placeholder="Separation distances, shared walls, wildfire/flood zone, site drainage..."></textarea>
        </div>
      </div>


    </div>`;
  }


  function addBuilding() {
    buildingCount++;
    const container = document.getElementById('additional-buildings-container');
    const div = document.createElement('div');
    div.id = `building-wrapper-${buildingCount}`;
    div.innerHTML = buildingCOPEHTML(buildingCount);
    container.appendChild(div);
    // Scroll to new building
    div.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
    showToast(`✓ Building ${buildingCount} added`);
  }


  function removeBuilding(num) {
    if (!confirm(`Remove Building ${num} and all its data?`)) return;
    const el = document.getElementById(`building-wrapper-${num}`);
    if (el) el.remove();
    showToast(`Building ${num} removed`);
  }


    // ── PUBLISH / UNPUBLISH REPORT ──
  async function togglePublishReport(id, isPublished, inspectionId, insuredName) {
    const action = isPublished ? 'unpublish' : 'publish';
    const msg = isPublished
      ? `Unpublish report for ${insuredName || inspectionId}? The client link will stop working.`
      : `Publish report for ${insuredName || inspectionId}? The client will be able to view it online using their reference number.`;


    if (!confirm(msg)) return;


    try {
      const { error } = await _supabase
        .from('inspections')
        .update({ report_published: !isPublished })
        .eq('id', id);


      if (error) throw error;


      if (!isPublished) {
        // Show the client link
        const link = `${window.location.origin}/report?ref=${inspectionId}`;
        showToast('✓ Report published — client link ready');
        // Show copyable link in a small prompt
        setTimeout(() => {
          if (confirm('Report published! Click OK to copy the client link to clipboard.')) {
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(link).then(() => showToast('✓ Link copied to clipboard'));
          }
        }, 400);
      } else {
        showToast('✓ Report unpublished — client link deactivated');
      }


      loadDashboard();
    } catch(e) {
      showToast('⚠ Failed to update: ' + (e.message || e), 'warn');
    }
  }


  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  // PORTAL SETTINGS — Access Code Management
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════


  async function showPortalSettings() {
    const wrap = document.getElementById('portal-settings-wrap');
    wrap.style.display = 'block';
    wrap.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });


    // Load current code from Supabase settings table
    const input = document.getElementById('portal-access-code-input');
    input.value = 'Loading...';
    input.disabled = true;


    try {
      const { data, error } = await _supabase
        .from('platform_settings')
        .select('value')
        .eq('key', 'portal_access_code')
        .single();


      input.disabled = false;
      if (error || !data) {
        // No code set yet — show the default
        input.value = 'Sanket2026';
      } else {
        input.value = data.value;
      }
    } catch(e) {
      input.disabled = false;
      input.value = 'Sanket2026';
      console.warn('Could not load access code:', e.message);
    }
  }


  async function saveAccessCode() {
    const input = document.getElementById('portal-access-code-input');
    const msg   = document.getElementById('access-code-msg');
    const newCode = input.value.trim();


    if (!newCode) {
      msg.textContent = '⚠ Please enter a code before saving.';
      msg.style.color = '#e53e3e';
      msg.style.display = 'block';
      return;
    }


    msg.textContent = '⏳ Saving...';
    msg.style.color = 'var(--slate)';
    msg.style.display = 'block';


    try {
      // Upsert — insert if not exists, update if it does
      const { error } = await _supabase
        .from('platform_settings')
        .upsert({ key: 'portal_access_code', value: newCode }, { onConflict: 'key' });


      if (error) throw error;


      msg.textContent = '✓ Access code updated successfully. New code is live immediately.';
      msg.style.color = '#276749';
      showToast('✓ Portal access code updated to: ' + newCode);


    } catch(e) {
      msg.textContent = '⚠ Failed to save: ' + (e.message || 'Please try again.');
      msg.style.color = '#e53e3e';
      console.error(e);
    }
  }


    // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  // SPRINKLER GRADE CALCULATOR
  // Based on SRC methodology + NFPA 25 deficiency scoring
  // Starting score = 100, demerits reduce score, score maps to Grade 1-5
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  function calculateSprinklerGrade() {
    const demeritFields = [
      'spk-hazard-class', 'spk-design-match', 'spk-qod',
      'spk-content-comb', 'spk-ceiling', 'spk-obstruction',
      'spk-openings', 'spk-internal-exp',
      'spk-water-adequacy', 'spk-connections', 'spk-valve-access',
      'spk-drain-drop', 'spk-head-condition', 'spk-piping',
      'spk-riser-heat', 'spk-fdc', 'spk-monitoring',
      'spk-annual-insp', 'spk-pump-test', 'spk-trip-test',
      'spk-5yr-insp', 'spk-underground-test', 'spk-impairments'
    ];


    // Check all fields have been completed
    var incomplete = [];
    var fieldLabels = {
      'spk-hazard-class':'Occupancy Hazard Classification',
      'spk-design-match':'System Design vs. Occupancy',
      'spk-qod':'Dry Pipe QOD Trip Time',
      'spk-content-comb':'Combustibility of Contents',
      'spk-ceiling':'High Ceiling / Storage Clearance',
      'spk-obstruction':'Sprinkler Obstruction',
      'spk-openings':'Unprotected Vertical Openings',
      'spk-internal-exp':'Internal Exposure',
      'spk-water-adequacy':'Water Supply Adequacy',
      'spk-connections':'Water Supply Connections',
      'spk-valve-access':'Control Valve Accessibility',
      'spk-drain-drop':'Pressure Drop on 2" Drain Test',
      'spk-head-condition':'Sprinkler Head Condition',
      'spk-piping':'Piping Condition',
      'spk-riser-heat':'Riser Room Heating',
      'spk-fdc':'Fire Department Connection',
      'spk-monitoring':'Central Station Monitoring',
      'spk-annual-insp':'Annual Inspection Currency',
      'spk-pump-test':'Fire Pump Annual Test',
      'spk-trip-test':'Dry Pipe / Deluge Valve Trip Test',
      'spk-5yr-insp':'5-Year Internal Obstruction Inspection',
      'spk-underground-test':'Underground Acceptance Testing',
      'spk-impairments':'Open Impairments'
    };


    demeritFields.forEach(id => {
      const el = document.getElementById(id);
      if (el && el.value === '') incomplete.push(fieldLabels[id] || id);
    });


    if (incomplete.length > 0) {
      showToast('⚠ Please complete all fields before calculating: ' + incomplete.slice(0,3).join(', ') + (incomplete.length > 3 ? ' + ' + (incomplete.length-3) + ' more' : ''), 'warn');
      return;
    }


    let totalDemerits = 0;
    demeritFields.forEach(id => {
      const el = document.getElementById(id);
      if (el && el.value !== '' && !isNaN(parseInt(el.value))) {
        totalDemerits += parseInt(el.value);
      }
    });


    // Cap demerits at 100
    totalDemerits = Math.min(totalDemerits, 100);
    const score = Math.max(0, 100 - totalDemerits);


    // Map score to grade
    let grade, gradeDesc, gradeColor;
    if (score >= 90) {
      grade = 1;
      gradeDesc = 'Grade 1 — Fully Effective: Water supply adequate, design matches occupancy, NFPA 25 current, ULC monitored. Maximum sprinkler credit applicable.';
      gradeColor = '#276749';
    } else if (score >= 75) {
      grade = 2;
      gradeDesc = 'Grade 2 — Effective with Minor Deficiencies: One or two non-critical items outstanding. Full sprinkler credit with recommendations noted.';
      gradeColor = '#7B5E00';
    } else if (score >= 55) {
      grade = 3;
      gradeDesc = 'Grade 3 — Partially Effective: Moderate deficiencies in design, coverage, or maintenance. Reduced credit — 30/90-day recommendations required.';
      gradeColor = '#C05621';
    } else if (score >= 35) {
      grade = 4;
      gradeDesc = 'Grade 4 — Marginally Effective: Significant deficiencies across multiple areas. Minimal credit — Immediate recommendations, refer to underwriter.';
      gradeColor = '#C53030';
    } else {
      grade = 5;
      gradeDesc = 'Grade 5 — Ineffective / Compromised: System impaired, water critically inadequate, or severely underdesigned for hazard. No sprinkler credit — treat as unprotected.';
      gradeColor = '#C53030';
    }


    // Update display
    document.getElementById('spk-demerit-total').textContent = totalDemerits;
    document.getElementById('spk-score').textContent = score;
    const gradeDisplay = document.getElementById('spk-grade-display');
    gradeDisplay.textContent = 'Grade ' + grade;
    gradeDisplay.style.color = gradeColor;
    document.getElementById('spk-grade-desc').textContent = gradeDesc;


    // Auto-set the final grade dropdown
    const finalSel = document.getElementById('spk-final-grade');
    if (finalSel) finalSel.value = String(grade);


    showToast('✓ Sprinkler Grade calculated: Grade ' + grade + ' (Score: ' + score + '/100)');
  }


    // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  // RECOMMENDATIONS LIBRARY — Supabase search & insert
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  let recLibraryData = [];      // cached from Supabase
  let recLibraryLoaded = false;


  async function openRecLibrary() {
    document.getElementById('rec-library-overlay').classList.add('open');
    document.getElementById('rec-lib-search').focus();
    if (!recLibraryLoaded) {
      await loadRecLibrary();
    } else {
      filterRecLibrary();
    }
  }


  function closeRecLibrary(e) {
    if (e && e.target !== document.getElementById('rec-library-overlay')) return;
    document.getElementById('rec-library-overlay').classList.remove('open');
  }


  async function loadRecLibrary() {
    const resultsEl = document.getElementById('rec-lib-results');
    resultsEl.innerHTML = '<div class="rec-lib-empty">⏳ Loading recommendations from database...</div>';


    try {
      const { data, error } = await _supabase
        .from('recommendations')
        .select('rec_id, category, subcategory, priority, responsible_party, title, rec_text')
        .eq('active', true)
        .order('category')
        .order('priority');


      if (error) {
        console.error('Supabase error:', JSON.stringify(error));
        throw error;
      }


      recLibraryData = data || [];
      recLibraryLoaded = true;
      console.log('Loaded ' + recLibraryData.length + ' recommendations');
      filterRecLibrary();
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Rec library load error:', err.message || err);
      resultsEl.innerHTML = '<div class="rec-lib-empty">⚠️ ' + (err.message || 'Could not load recommendations library. Check your connection and try again.') + '</div>';
    }
  }


  function filterRecLibrary() {
    const query    = (document.getElementById('rec-lib-search').value || '').toLowerCase().trim();
    const catFilter  = document.getElementById('rec-lib-cat').value;
    const prioFilter = document.getElementById('rec-lib-prio').value;
    const resultsEl  = document.getElementById('rec-lib-results');
    const countEl    = document.getElementById('rec-lib-count');


    let filtered = recLibraryData;


    if (catFilter)  filtered = filtered.filter(r => r.category === catFilter);
    if (prioFilter) filtered = filtered.filter(r => r.priority === prioFilter);
    if (query) {
      filtered = filtered.filter(r =>
        (r.title    || '').toLowerCase().includes(query) ||
        (r.rec_text || '').toLowerCase().includes(query) ||
        (r.category || '').toLowerCase().includes(query) ||
        (r.subcategory || '').toLowerCase().includes(query)
      );
    }


    // Default: show all if no filters set
    if (!query && !catFilter && !prioFilter) {
      filtered = recLibraryData;
    }


    countEl.textContent = filtered.length + ' of ' + recLibraryData.length + ' recommendations';


    if (filtered.length === 0) {
      resultsEl.innerHTML = '<div class="rec-lib-empty">No recommendations match your search. Try a different keyword or clear the filters.</div>';
      return;
    }


    resultsEl.innerHTML = filtered.map(function(r) {
      var prioClass = (r.priority || '').replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9-]/g,'');
      var preview   = (r.rec_text || '').substring(0, 200);
      if (r.rec_text && r.rec_text.length > 200) preview += '...';
      var safeTitle = (r.title    || '').replace(/"/g, '&quot;').replace(/'/g, '&#39;');
      var safeText  = (r.rec_text || '').replace(/"/g, '&quot;').replace(/'/g, '&#39;');
      var safePrio  = (r.priority  || '').replace(/"/g, '&quot;').replace(/'/g, '&#39;');
      var safeCat   = (r.category  || '').replace(/"/g, '&quot;').replace(/'/g, '&#39;');
      return '<div class="rec-lib-item prio-' + prioClass + '">' +
        '<div class="rec-lib-item-header">' +
          '<span class="rec-lib-badge badge-' + prioClass + '">' + (r.priority || '') + '</span>' +
          '<span class="rec-lib-title">' + (r.title || '') + '</span>' +
          '<span class="rec-lib-cat">' + (r.subcategory || r.category || '') + '</span>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div class="rec-lib-preview">' + preview + '</div>' +
        '<button class="rec-lib-insert-btn" ' +
          'onclick=\'insertRecFromLibrary(this)\' ' +
          'data-title="' + safeTitle + '" ' +
          'data-text="'  + safeText  + '" ' +
          'data-prio="'  + safePrio  + '" ' +
          'data-cat="'   + safeCat   + '">' +
          '&#xff0b; Insert' +
        '</button>' +
        '<div style="clear:both"></div>' +
      '</div>';
    }).join('');
  }


  function insertRecFromLibrary(btn) {
    var title    = (btn.getAttribute('data-title') || '').replace(/&quot;/g,'"').replace(/&#39;/g,"'");
    var text     = (btn.getAttribute('data-text')  || '').replace(/&quot;/g,'"').replace(/&#39;/g,"'");
    var priority = btn.getAttribute('data-prio')  || '';
    var category = btn.getAttribute('data-cat')   || '';


    var prioMap = { 'Immediate': 'high', '30-Day': 'high', '90-Day': 'med', 'Advisory': 'low' };
    var level = prioMap[priority] || 'med';


    // If rec-1 textarea is empty, populate it instead of creating rec-2
    var rec1 = document.getElementById('rec-1');
    if (rec1) {
      var rec1ta = rec1.querySelector('textarea');
      if (rec1ta && !rec1ta.value.trim()) {
        rec1ta.value = text;
        // Pre-fill title field with library rec title
        var rec1title = rec1.querySelector('.rec-title-field');
        if (rec1title && title) rec1title.value = title;
        // Set priority
        rec1.className = 'rec-item priority-' + level;
        var priorityLbl = rec1.querySelector('[data-level="' + level + '"]');
        if (priorityLbl) setRecPriority(priorityLbl, 'rec-1', level);
        // Add delete button if not already there
        addDeleteBtn(rec1);
        document.getElementById('rec-library-overlay').classList.remove('open');
        showToast('Recommendation inserted into #1: ' + title.substring(0, 50));
        setTimeout(function() { rec1.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' }); }, 200);
        return;
      }
    }


    recCount++;
    var div = document.createElement('div');
    div.className = 'rec-item priority-' + level;
    div.id = 'rec-' + recCount;


    var catToSection = {
      'Fire Protection': 'Protection — Fire',
      'Electrical': 'Construction',
      'Life Safety': 'Protection — Fire',
      'Premises Liability': 'Other',
      'Housekeeping': 'Housekeeping',
      'Safety & Compliance': 'Safety / Compliance',
      'Security': 'Protection — Security',
      'Spray Finishing': 'Occupancy',
      'Heating Systems': 'Construction',
      'Flammable & Combustible Liquids': 'Occupancy',
      'Structural & Water Damage': 'Construction',
      'Warehouse & Storage': 'Occupancy',
      'Woodworking Operations': 'Occupancy',
      'Auto Service': 'Occupancy',
      'Fleet Safety': 'Other',
      'Building Systems': 'Construction',
      'Pool, Playground & Amenities': 'Other',
      'Multi-Residential': 'Occupancy',
      'Contractors & Administration': 'Other'
    };
    var sectionVal = catToSection[category] || 'Other';
    var sectionOptions = ['Construction','Occupancy','Protection — Fire','Protection — Security','Exposure','Safety / Compliance','Housekeeping','Other'];
    var sectionOpts = sectionOptions.map(function(o) {
      return '<option' + (o === sectionVal ? ' selected' : '') + '>' + o + '</option>';
    }).join('');


    var hHigh = level === 'high' ? ' selected' : '';
    var hMed  = level === 'med'  ? ' selected' : '';
    var hLow  = level === 'low'  ? ' selected' : '';
    var rc = recCount;


    div.innerHTML =
      '<div class="rec-header">' +
        '<span class="rec-num">#' + rc + '</span>' +
        '<div class="radio-group" style="flex-wrap:nowrap;gap:6px">' +
          '<label class="radio-btn' + hHigh + '" style="padding:4px 10px;font-size:11px" data-level="high" data-rec="rec-' + rc + '">High</label>' +
          '<label class="radio-btn' + hMed  + '" style="padding:4px 10px;font-size:11px" data-level="med"  data-rec="rec-' + rc + '">Medium</label>' +
          '<label class="radio-btn' + hLow  + '" style="padding:4px 10px;font-size:11px" data-level="low"  data-rec="rec-' + rc + '">Low</label>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<select style="margin-left:auto;width:160px;font-size:12px"><option>Requirement</option><option>Recommendation</option></select>' +
      '</div>' +
      '<div class="form-grid">' +
        '<div class="field"><label>Reference Number</label>' +
          '<input type="text" class="rec-ref-field" placeholder="e.g. 2026-03-001" style="font-family:IBM Plex Mono,monospace;font-weight:700;color:var(--navy);"></div>' +
        '<div class="field form-full"><label>Brief Title / Heading</label>' +
          '<input type="text" class="rec-title-field" placeholder="e.g. Sprinkler system overdue for annual inspection"></div>' +
        '<div class="field form-full"><label>Description of Deficiency / Recommendation</label>' +
          '<textarea style="min-height:100px"></textarea>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div class="field"><label>Section / Area</label>' +
          '<select><option value="">— Select —</option>' + sectionOpts + '</select>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div class="field"><label>Compliance Deadline</label><input type="date"></div>' +
        '<div class="field"><label>Follow-Up Required?</label>' +
          '<select><option>Yes — Re-inspection</option><option>Yes — Documentation only</option><option>No</option></select>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div class="field"><label>Consequence if Not Corrected</label>' +
          '<select><option value="">— Select —</option>' +
            '<option>Premium surcharge</option><option>Coverage restriction</option>' +
            '<option>Cancellation / Non-renewal</option><option>Informational only</option>' +
          '</select>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div class="field form-full"><label>Inspector Notes / Remarks</label>' +
          '<textarea class="rec-notes-field" placeholder="e.g. Insured advised — target date March 31. Landlord responsibility per lease..."></textarea>' +
        '</div>' +
      '</div>';


    // Wire up priority buttons via event delegation
    div.querySelectorAll('[data-level]').forEach(function(lbl) {
      lbl.addEventListener('click', function() {
        setRecPriority(this, this.getAttribute('data-rec'), this.getAttribute('data-level'));
      });
    });


    // Set textarea value safely after DOM insertion
    div.querySelector('textarea').value = text;
    // Pre-fill title from library entry title
    var titleInput = div.querySelector('.rec-title-field');
    if (titleInput && title) titleInput.value = title;


    // Add delete button
    addDeleteBtn(div);


    document.getElementById('rec-list').appendChild(div);
    document.getElementById('rec-library-overlay').classList.remove('open');
    showToast('Recommendation inserted — #' + rc + ': ' + title.substring(0, 50));
    setTimeout(function() { div.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' }); }, 200);
  }


  function addDeleteBtn(recDiv) {
    // Don't add if already has one
    if (recDiv.querySelector('.rec-delete-btn')) return;
    var header = recDiv.querySelector('.rec-header');
    if (!header) return;
    var btn = document.createElement('button');
    btn.className = 'rec-delete-btn';
    btn.title = 'Remove this recommendation';
    btn.innerHTML = '&#x1F5D1;';
    btn.style.cssText = 'background:none;border:none;cursor:pointer;font-size:15px;color:#C53030;padding:2px 4px;margin-left:6px;opacity:0.7;line-height:1;';
    btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
      if (confirm('Remove this recommendation?')) {
        recDiv.remove();
        // Renumber remaining recs
        document.querySelectorAll('#rec-list .rec-item').forEach(function(item, idx) {
          var numEl = item.querySelector('.rec-num');
          if (numEl) numEl.textContent = '#' + (idx + 1);
        });
        recCount = document.querySelectorAll('#rec-list .rec-item').length;
      }
    });
    btn.addEventListener('mouseover', function() { this.style.opacity = '1'; });
    btn.addEventListener('mouseout',  function() { this.style.opacity = '0.7'; });
    header.appendChild(btn);
  }


  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  // INTERIOR FINISHES — Dynamic rows
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  var FLOOR_OPTIONS = ['Concrete — Sealed','Concrete — Bare','Ceramic / Porcelain Tile','Hardwood','Engineered Wood','Laminate','Vinyl / LVP','Carpet','Epoxy Coating','Terrazzo','Stone / Marble','Anti-Static / Raised','Other'];
  var WALL_OPTIONS  = ['Drywall / Gypsum Board','Plaster','Brick — Exposed Interior','Concrete Block (CMU)','Concrete — Poured','Metal Panel / Liner Panel','Wood Panelling','Ceramic / Porcelain Tile','Glass / Curtainwall','Acoustic Panel','Paint on Masonry','Other'];
  var CEIL_OPTIONS  = ['Suspended T-Bar / Acoustic Tile','Drywall / Gypsum Board','Plaster','Exposed — Open Structure (Steel)','Exposed — Open Structure (Wood)','Concrete — Exposed','Metal Deck — Exposed','Wood — Tongue & Groove','Spray Fireproofing','Other'];


  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  // PHOTO STORAGE — Supabase Storage + metadata
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════


  async function savePhotoMetadata() {
    if (!currentInspectionId) return;
    var photos = [];
    for (var i = 1; i <= photoCount; i++) {
      var img = document.getElementById('photo-' + i + '-img');
      if (!img || !img.classList.contains('loaded')) continue;
      var caption  = document.getElementById('photo-' + i + '-caption');
      var category = document.getElementById('photo-' + i + '-category');
      var storagePath = img.getAttribute('data-storage-path') || '';
      photos.push({
        num:      i,
        caption:  caption  ? caption.value  : '',
        category: category ? category.value : '',
        path:     storagePath
      });
    }
    if (!photos.length) return;
    // Save as JSON column on the inspection record
    try {
      await _supabase.from('inspections')
        .update({ photo_data: JSON.stringify(photos) })
        .eq('id', currentInspectionId);
    } catch(e) {
      console.warn('Photo metadata save failed:', e.message);
    }
  }


  async function loadPhotosFromStorage(photoData) {
    if (!photoData) return;
    var photos = [];
    try { photos = JSON.parse(photoData); } catch(e) { return; }
    if (!photos.length) return;


    for (var i = 0; i < photos.length; i++) {
      var p = photos[i];
      if (!p.num || !p.path) continue;


      // Ensure the photo slot exists
      while (photoCount < p.num) addPhotoSlot();


      // Get a signed URL from Supabase Storage
      try {
        var imgEl      = document.getElementById('photo-' + p.num + '-img');
        var phEl       = document.getElementById('photo-' + p.num + '-placeholder');
        var captionEl  = document.getElementById('photo-' + p.num + '-caption');
        var categoryEl = document.getElementById('photo-' + p.num + '-category');


        var { data: urlData, error: urlErr } = await _supabase.storage
          .from('inspection-photos')
          .createSignedUrl(p.path, 3600); // 1 hour signed URL


        if (!urlErr && urlData && imgEl) {
          imgEl.src = urlData.signedUrl;
          imgEl.classList.add('loaded');
          imgEl.setAttribute('data-storage-path', p.path);
          if (phEl) phEl.style.display = 'none';
        }
        if (captionEl  && p.caption)  captionEl.value  = p.caption;
        if (categoryEl && p.category) categoryEl.value = p.category;
      } catch(e) {
        console.warn('Could not load photo ' + p.num + ' from storage:', e.message);
      }
    }
  }


    // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  // QA WORKFLOW — Status management, locking, transitions
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════


  // ── RESET QA TO DRAFT (admin only) ──
  async function resetQAToDraft() {
    if (currentUserRole !== 'admin') return;
    if (!currentInspectionId) { showToast('No inspection loaded.', 'warn'); return; }
    var inspId = document.getElementById('inspection-id') ? document.getElementById('inspection-id').value : currentInspectionId;
    if (!confirm('Reset ' + inspId + ' to Draft status?\nReviewer assignment will be cleared.')) return;
    try {
      var { error } = await _supabase.from('inspections')
        .update({ report_status: 'draft', qa_reviewer: null, qa_notes: null, qa_date: null })
        .eq('id', currentInspectionId);
      if (error) throw error;
      currentReportStatus = 'draft';
      currentQAReviewer = '';
      currentQANotes = '';
      currentQADate = '';
      var nameEl = document.getElementById('qa-reviewer-name');
      if (nameEl) nameEl.value = '';
      var btnSubmit = document.getElementById('btn-submit-qa');
      if (btnSubmit) btnSubmit.textContent = '📋 Submit for QA Review';
      applyQAState('draft');
      showToast('✓ Reset to Draft — reviewer cleared.');
    } catch(e) {
      showToast('⚠ Reset failed: ' + e.message, 'warn');
    }
  }


  // ── ASSIGN TO REVIEWER (from dashboard) ──
  async function assignToReviewer(dbId, reviewerName) {
    if (!reviewerName) return;
    if (!confirm('Assign this report to ' + reviewerName + ' for QA review?\nStatus will change to In Review.')) {
      // Reset dropdown
      var sel = document.getElementById('assign-qa-' + dbId);
      if (sel) sel.value = '';
      return;
    }
    try {
      var { error } = await _supabase.from('inspections')
        .update({ report_status: 'inreview', qa_reviewer: reviewerName })
        .eq('id', dbId);
      if (error) throw error;
      showToast('✓ Assigned to ' + reviewerName + ' — status set to In Review.');
      // If this is the currently loaded inspection, update local state
      if (currentInspectionId === dbId) {
        currentReportStatus = 'inreview';
        currentQAReviewer   = reviewerName;
        applyQAState('inreview');
        var nameEl = document.getElementById('qa-reviewer-name');
        if (nameEl) nameEl.value = reviewerName;
      }
      loadDashboard();
    } catch(e) {
      showToast('⚠ Assignment failed: ' + e.message, 'warn');
    }
  }


  // ── ADMIN UNLOCK ──
  async function adminUnlockInspection(dbId, inspId) {
    if (currentUserRole !== 'admin' && currentUserRole !== 'reviewer') {
      showToast('⚠ Only admins and reviewers can unlock files.', 'warn'); return;
    }
    var label = inspId || dbId;
    if (!confirm('Unlock inspection ' + label + ' and reset to Draft?\n\nThe QA reviewer assignment will be cleared.')) return;
    try {
      var { error } = await _supabase.from('inspections')
        .update({ report_status: 'draft', qa_reviewer: null, qa_notes: null, qa_date: null })
        .eq('id', dbId);
      if (error) throw error;
      showToast('✓ Inspection ' + label + ' unlocked — status reset to Draft.');
      // If this is the currently loaded inspection, update local state too
      if (currentInspectionId === dbId) {
        currentReportStatus = 'draft';
        currentQAReviewer   = '';
        currentQANotes      = '';
        currentQADate       = '';
        applyQAState('draft');
      }
      loadDashboard();
    } catch(e) {
      showToast('⚠ Unlock failed: ' + e.message, 'warn');
    }
  }


  // QA statuses: draft | submitted | inreview | returned | approved
  var currentReportStatus = 'draft';
  var currentQAReviewer   = '';
  var qaReviewerList      = []; // loaded from profiles


  // Load reviewer list (admin + reviewer roles)
  async function loadReviewerList() {
    try {
      var { data, error } = await _supabase
        .from('profiles')
        .select('id, full_name, email, role')
        .in('role', ['admin', 'reviewer'])
        .order('full_name');
      if (!error && data) qaReviewerList = data;
    } catch(e) { console.warn('Could not load reviewer list:', e.message); }
  }


  // Apply visual state based on status and current user role
  function applyQAState(status) {
    currentReportStatus = status || 'draft';
    var isReviewer = (currentUserRole === 'admin' || currentUserRole === 'reviewer');


    var summaryPanel = document.getElementById('section-summary');


    var banner      = document.getElementById('qa-status-banner');
    var pill        = document.getElementById('qa-status-pill');
    var btnSubmit   = document.getElementById('btn-submit-qa');
    var btnExport   = document.getElementById('report-btn-group');
    var btnSave     = document.getElementById('btn-save-db');
    var qaMsg       = document.getElementById('qa-status-message');
    var qaActions   = document.getElementById('qa-action-buttons');
    var qaApproved  = document.getElementById('qa-approved-section');
    var qaReturned  = document.getElementById('qa-returned-section');
    var nameEl      = document.getElementById('qa-reviewer-name');
    var dateEl      = document.getElementById('qa-review-date');
    var notesEl     = document.getElementById('qa-notes');
    var returnNotes = document.getElementById('qa-return-notes-display');
    var approvedBy  = document.getElementById('qa-approved-by-label');


    // Hide conditional sections by default
    if (qaApproved) qaApproved.style.display = 'none';
    if (qaReturned) qaReturned.style.display = 'none';


    // Populate reviewer fields
    if (nameEl) nameEl.value = currentQAReviewer || '';
    if (notesEl && currentQANotes) notesEl.value = currentQANotes;


    if (currentReportStatus === 'draft') {
      if (banner) { banner.className = 'qa-status-banner'; banner.textContent = ''; }
      if (pill)   { pill.className = 'qa-status-pill qa-pill-draft'; pill.textContent = 'Draft'; }
      if (btnSubmit) btnSubmit.disabled = false;
      if (btnSave)   btnSave.style.display = 'inline-block';
      if (btnExport) btnExport.style.display = 'flex';
      if (qaMsg)  qaMsg.textContent = 'Submit the report for QA review when complete.';
      if (qaActions) qaActions.style.display = 'none';
      var btnReset0 = document.getElementById('btn-qa-reset');
      if (btnReset0) btnReset0.style.display = 'none';
      // Pre-fill reviewer name with logged-in user if they are a reviewer
      if (isReviewer && nameEl && !nameEl.value) {
        var found = qaReviewerList.find(function(r) { return r.email === currentUserEmail; });
        if (found) nameEl.value = found.full_name || found.email;
      }


    } else if (currentReportStatus === 'submitted') {
      if (banner) { banner.className = 'qa-status-banner qa-banner-submitted'; banner.textContent = isReviewer ? '⏳ Submitted — Assign from dashboard or complete review below.' : '⏳ Submitted for QA Review. You will be notified when complete.'; }
      if (pill)   { pill.className = 'qa-status-pill qa-pill-submitted'; pill.textContent = 'Submitted'; }
      if (btnSubmit) { btnSubmit.disabled = true; btnSubmit.textContent = '⏳ Under QA Review'; btnSubmit.style.background = '#b8962f'; btnSubmit.style.opacity = '0.7'; btnSubmit.style.cursor = 'not-allowed'; }
      if (btnSave)   btnSave.style.display = isReviewer ? 'inline-block' : 'none';
      if (btnExport) btnExport.style.display = 'flex';
      if (qaMsg)  qaMsg.textContent = isReviewer ? 'This report is awaiting QA review. Complete your review below.' : 'Report locked pending QA review.';
      var btnReset = document.getElementById('btn-qa-reset');
      if (btnReset) btnReset.style.display = (currentUserRole === 'admin') ? 'inline-block' : 'none';
      if (isReviewer) {
        if (qaActions) { qaActions.style.display = 'flex'; }
        if (dateEl && !dateEl.value) dateEl.value = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
      }


    } else if (currentReportStatus === 'inreview') {
      if (banner) { banner.className = 'qa-status-banner qa-banner-inreview'; banner.textContent = isReviewer ? '🔍 In QA Review — Reviewer: ' + (currentQAReviewer || 'Assigned') + '. Complete your review below.' : '🔍 In QA Review — Reviewer: ' + (currentQAReviewer || 'Assigned') + '. Your report is locked pending review.'; }
      if (pill)   { pill.className = 'qa-status-pill qa-pill-inreview'; pill.textContent = 'In Review'; }
      if (btnSubmit) { btnSubmit.disabled = true; btnSubmit.textContent = '🔍 Under QA Review'; btnSubmit.style.background = '#7c6fb5'; btnSubmit.style.color = 'white'; btnSubmit.style.opacity = '0.7'; btnSubmit.style.cursor = 'not-allowed'; }
      if (btnSave)   btnSave.style.display = isReviewer ? 'inline-block' : 'none';
      if (btnExport) btnExport.style.display = 'flex';
      if (qaMsg)  qaMsg.textContent = isReviewer ? 'Review the report and approve or return for correction.' : 'Your report is being reviewed.';
      var btnReset2 = document.getElementById('btn-qa-reset');
      if (btnReset2) btnReset2.style.display = (currentUserRole === 'admin') ? 'inline-block' : 'none';
      if (isReviewer) {
        if (qaActions) { qaActions.style.display = 'flex'; }
        if (dateEl && !dateEl.value) dateEl.value = currentQADate || new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
      }


    } else if (currentReportStatus === 'returned') {
      if (banner) { banner.className = 'qa-status-banner qa-banner-returned'; banner.textContent = '↩ Returned for Correction — Please review the QA notes and resubmit when ready.'; }
      if (pill)   { pill.className = 'qa-status-pill qa-pill-returned'; pill.textContent = 'Returned'; }
      if (btnSubmit) { btnSubmit.disabled = false; btnSubmit.textContent = '📋 Submit for QA Review'; btnSubmit.style.background = 'var(--gold)'; btnSubmit.style.color = 'var(--navy)'; btnSubmit.style.opacity = '1'; btnSubmit.style.cursor = 'pointer'; btnSubmit.textContent = '📋 Resubmit for QA Review'; }
      if (btnSave)   btnSave.style.display = 'inline-block';
      if (btnExport) btnExport.style.display = 'flex';
      if (qaMsg)  qaMsg.textContent = 'This report has been returned. Review the notes below and resubmit.';
      if (qaReturned) {
        qaReturned.style.display = 'block';
        if (returnNotes) returnNotes.textContent = currentQANotes || 'No specific notes provided.';
      }


    } else if (currentReportStatus === 'approved') {
      if (banner) { banner.className = 'qa-status-banner qa-banner-approved'; banner.textContent = '✅ QA Approved — Report is approved and ready for printing.'; }
      if (pill)   { pill.className = 'qa-status-pill qa-pill-approved'; pill.textContent = 'Approved'; }
      if (btnSubmit) { btnSubmit.disabled = true; btnSubmit.textContent = '✅ Review Completed'; btnSubmit.style.background = '#276749'; btnSubmit.style.color = 'white'; btnSubmit.style.opacity = '1'; btnSubmit.style.cursor = 'not-allowed'; }
      // Show reset button for admin even in approved state
      var btnResetApproved = document.getElementById('btn-qa-reset');
      if (btnResetApproved) btnResetApproved.style.display = (currentUserRole === 'admin') ? 'inline-block' : 'none';
      if (btnSave)   btnSave.style.display = isReviewer ? 'inline-block' : 'none';
      if (btnExport) btnExport.style.display = 'flex';
      if (qaMsg)  qaMsg.textContent = 'This report has been approved.';
      if (qaActions) qaActions.style.display = 'none';
      if (qaApproved) {
        qaApproved.style.display = 'block';
        if (approvedBy) approvedBy.textContent = 'Approved by ' + (currentQAReviewer || '—') + ' on ' + (currentQADate || '—');
      }
    }




  }


  var currentQANotes = '';
  var currentQADate  = '';


  // Submit for QA
  async function submitForQA() {
    if (!currentInspectionId) {
      showToast('⚠ Please save the inspection first before submitting for QA.', 'warn'); return;
    }
    var msg = 'Submit this report for QA Review?' +
              '\n\nWARNING: Once submitted, you will not be able to edit this report ' +
              'until the reviewer returns it for correction.' +
              '\n\nMake sure you have saved all your work first.';
    if (!confirm(msg)) return;


    // Auto-fill signature and submission date if empty
    var sigEl  = document.getElementById('inspector-signature');
    var dateEl = document.getElementById('date-submitted');
    if (sigEl && !sigEl.value && currentUserEmail) sigEl.value = currentUserEmail;
    if (dateEl && !dateEl.value) dateEl.value = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];


    await saveInspection(); // Save current state first
    try {
      var { error } = await _supabase.from('inspections')
        .update({ report_status: 'submitted', qa_reviewer: null, qa_notes: null, qa_date: null })
        .eq('id', currentInspectionId);
      if (error) throw error;
      currentReportStatus = 'submitted';
      applyQAState('submitted');
      showToast('✓ Report submitted for QA review.');
      // Scroll QA card into view so user sees the status change
      setTimeout(function() {
        var qaCard = document.getElementById('qa-review-card');
        if (qaCard) qaCard.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
      }, 300);
    } catch(e) {
      showToast('⚠ Submit failed: ' + e.message, 'warn');
    }
  }


  // Reviewer claims the file
  async function claimQAReview() {
    if (!currentInspectionId) return;
    var reviewerName = '';
    // Use full name from profiles if available
    if (currentUserEmail) {
      var found = qaReviewerList.find(function(r) { return r.email === currentUserEmail; });
      reviewerName = found ? (found.full_name || found.email) : currentUserEmail;
    }
    try {
      var { error } = await _supabase.from('inspections')
        .update({ report_status: 'inreview', qa_reviewer: reviewerName })
        .eq('id', currentInspectionId);
      if (error) throw error;
      currentReportStatus = 'inreview';
      currentQAReviewer   = reviewerName;
      // Pre-fill reviewer name field
      var nameEl = document.getElementById('qa-reviewer-name');
      if (nameEl) nameEl.value = reviewerName;
      var dateEl = document.getElementById('qa-review-date');
      if (dateEl) dateEl.value = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
      applyQAState('inreview');
      showToast('✓ File claimed — you are now the assigned reviewer.');
    } catch(e) {
      showToast('⚠ Could not claim file: ' + e.message, 'warn');
    }
  }


  // Reviewer approves
  async function approveQA() {
    if (!currentInspectionId) return;
    var notes    = document.getElementById('qa-notes')?.value || '';
    var dateVal  = document.getElementById('qa-review-date')?.value || new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
    if (!confirm('Approve this report? The Export PDF button will become available.')) return;
    try {
      var { error } = await _supabase.from('inspections')
        .update({ report_status: 'approved', qa_notes: notes, qa_date: dateVal })
        .eq('id', currentInspectionId);
      if (error) throw error;
      currentReportStatus = 'approved';
      currentQANotes = notes;
      currentQADate  = dateVal;
      applyQAState('approved');
      showToast('✓ Report approved — Export PDF is now available.');
    } catch(e) {
      showToast('⚠ Approval failed: ' + e.message, 'warn');
    }
  }


  // Reviewer returns for correction
  async function returnForCorrection() {
    if (!currentInspectionId) return;
    var notes = document.getElementById('qa-notes')?.value || '';
    if (!notes.trim()) {
      showToast('⚠ Please add QA notes explaining what needs to be corrected.', 'warn'); return;
    }
    if (!confirm('Return this report to the inspector for correction?')) return;
    try {
      var { error } = await _supabase.from('inspections')
        .update({ report_status: 'returned', qa_notes: notes, qa_date: new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] })
        .eq('id', currentInspectionId);
      if (error) throw error;
      currentReportStatus = 'returned';
      currentQANotes = notes;
      applyQAState('returned');
      showToast('↩ Report returned to inspector for correction.');
    } catch(e) {
      showToast('⚠ Return failed: ' + e.message, 'warn');
    }
  }


    // ── PERCENTAGE ROW HELPERS (wall, roof, heating, AC) ──
  var PCT_OPTIONS = {
    wall:  ['Wood Frame','Brick / Masonry','Concrete Block (CMU)','Tilt-Up Concrete','Precast Concrete','Steel / Metal Panel','EIFS / Stucco','Glass Curtainwall','Mixed / Other'],
    roof:  ['EPDM / Single-Ply Membrane','TPO','Built-Up (BUR / Tar & Gravel)','Metal / Standing Seam','Asphalt Shingle','Tile (Clay / Concrete)','Slate','Modified Bitumen','Insulated Metal Panel','Other'],
    heat:  ['Gas Forced Air (Furnace)','Boiler — Hot Water','Boiler — Steam','Rooftop Unit (RTU) — Gas','Electric Baseboard','Radiant In-Floor','Heat Pump','District / Central Plant','Wood / Pellet','None','Other'],
    ac:    ['Central Air — Split System','Rooftop Unit (RTU)','Chilled Water System','Variable Refrigerant Flow (VRF)','Window / Packaged Terminal (PTAC)','Evaporative Cooling','Heat Pump','District / Central Plant','None','Other'],
    frame:    ['Wood Frame','Steel Frame','Reinforced Concrete','Load-Bearing Masonry','Pre-Engineered Metal','Hybrid / Mixed'],
    rooftype: ['Flat / Low Slope','Gable','Hip','Gambrel','Shed / Mono-Slope','Sawtooth / Industrial','Curved / Barrel'],
    deck:     ['Steel / Metal Deck','Wood / Plywood','Concrete — Poured','Concrete — Precast','Insulated Metal Panel (IMP)','Cementitious Wood Fibre'],
    extfinish:['Brick — Standard','Brick — Face / Decorative','Stone — Natural','Stone — Simulated / Manufactured','Stucco / EIFS','Glass Curtainwall','Architectural Precast Concrete','Exposed Concrete','Metal Cladding / Composite Panel','Vinyl Siding','Wood Siding','Fibre Cement Board','GFRC Panel','Other'],
    isoclass: ['Class 1 — Frame','Class 2 — Joisted Masonry','Class 3 — Non-Combustible / Masonry','Class 4 — Masonry Non-Combustible','Class 5 — Modified Fire Resistive','Class 6 — Fire Resistive'],
    bsmtuse:  ['Parking Garage — Open','Parking Garage — Enclosed','Storage / Warehouse','Mechanical / Utility','Retail / Commercial','Office','Residential Units','Crawl Space — Unoccupied','Crawl Space — Service Only','Industrial / Processing','Other']
  };


  function addPctRowTo(containerId, type) {
    var container = document.getElementById(containerId);
    if (!container) return;
    var options = PCT_OPTIONS[type] || [];
    var optHtml = '<option value="">— Select —</option>' + options.map(function(o) {
      return '<option>' + o + '</option>';
    }).join('');
    var row = document.createElement('div');
    row.className = 'pct-row';
    row.style.cssText = 'display:grid;grid-template-columns:2fr 1fr auto;gap:10px;align-items:center;margin-bottom:8px;';
    row.innerHTML =
      '<select style="font-family:inherit;font-size:13px;padding:7px 10px;border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:6px;">' + optHtml + '</select>' +
      '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:4px;">' +
        '<input type="number" min="0" max="100" placeholder="%" style="font-family:inherit;font-size:13px;padding:7px 8px;border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:6px;width:64px;">' +
        '<span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--slate);">%</span>' +
      '</div>' +
      '<button onclick="removePctRow(this)" style="background:none;border:none;color:#C53030;font-size:18px;cursor:pointer;padding:2px 4px;" title="Remove">&#x2715;</button>';
    container.appendChild(row);
  }


  function removePctRow(btn) {
    var row = btn.closest('.pct-row');
    if (row) row.remove();
  }


  function getOptionsForType(type) {
    if (type === 'wall')    return WALL_OPTIONS;
    if (type === 'ceiling') return CEIL_OPTIONS;
    return FLOOR_OPTIONS;
  }


  function addFinishRowTo(containerId, type) {
    var container = document.getElementById(containerId);
    if (!container) return;
    var options = getOptionsForType(type);
    var optHtml = '<option value="">— Material —</option>' + options.map(function(o) {
      return '<option>' + o + '</option>';
    }).join('');
    var row = document.createElement('div');
    row.className = 'finish-row';
    row.style.cssText = 'display:grid;grid-template-columns:2fr 2fr 1fr auto;gap:10px;align-items:center;margin-bottom:8px;';
    row.innerHTML =
      '<select style="font-family:inherit;font-size:13px;padding:7px 10px;border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:6px;">' + optHtml + '</select>' +
      '<input type="text" placeholder="Location / notes" style="font-family:inherit;font-size:13px;padding:7px 10px;border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:6px;">' +
      '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:4px;">' +
        '<input type="number" min="0" max="100" placeholder="%" style="font-family:inherit;font-size:13px;padding:7px 8px;border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:6px;width:64px;">' +
        '<span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--slate);">%</span>' +
      '</div>' +
      '<button onclick="removeFinishRow(this)" style="background:none;border:none;color:#C53030;font-size:18px;cursor:pointer;padding:2px 4px;" title="Remove">&#x2715;</button>';
    container.appendChild(row);
  }


  function removeFinishRow(btn) {
    var row = btn.closest('.finish-row');
    if (row) row.remove();
  }


  function toggleBasementUse() {
    var area = parseFloat(document.getElementById('basement-area').value) || 0;
    var type = document.getElementById('basement-type') ? document.getElementById('basement-type').value : '';
    var section = document.getElementById('basement-use-section');
    if (section) {
      section.style.display = (area > 0 || (type && type !== 'None')) ? 'block' : 'none';
    }
  }


  function toggleMezzanine() {
    var val = document.getElementById('mezzanine-present').value;
    var details = document.getElementById('mezzanine-details');
    if (details) details.style.display = (val === 'Yes') ? 'block' : 'none';
  }


  function toggleElevDetails() {
    var p = parseInt(document.getElementById('elev-passenger-count').value) || 0;
    var f = parseInt(document.getElementById('elev-freight-count').value) || 0;
    var details = document.getElementById('elev-details');
    if (details) details.style.display = (p + f > 0) ? 'block' : 'none';
  }


  function initKeyboardNav() {
    // Add tabindex and Enter/Space activation to all radio-btn and check-btn labels
    document.querySelectorAll('.radio-btn, .check-btn').forEach(el => {
      el.setAttribute('tabindex', '0');
      el.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
        if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
          e.preventDefault();
          el.click();
        }
      });
    });


    // Use MutationObserver to catch dynamically added elements (e.g. design area cards)
    const observer = new MutationObserver(mutations => {
      mutations.forEach(m => {
        m.addedNodes.forEach(node => {
          if (node.nodeType !== 1) return;
          node.querySelectorAll && node.querySelectorAll('.radio-btn, .check-btn').forEach(el => {
            if (!el.getAttribute('tabindex')) {
              el.setAttribute('tabindex', '0');
              el.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
                if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
                  e.preventDefault();
                  el.click();
                }
              });
            }
          });
        });
      });
    });
    observer.observe(document.body, { childList: true, subtree: true });
  }


  // ── INIT ──
  // Initialize rec-1 priority button click handlers (static item)
  document.querySelectorAll('#rec-1 [data-level]').forEach(function(lbl) {
    lbl.addEventListener('click', function() {
      setRecPriority(this, this.getAttribute('data-rec'), this.getAttribute('data-level'));
    });
  });


  window._loadInProgress = false;
  document.getElementById('inspection-date').valueAsDate = new Date();
  // Restore action bar after printing (print CSS hides it)
  window.addEventListener('afterprint', function() {
    var ab = document.getElementById('action-bar');
    if (ab) ab.style.display = 'flex';
  });
  updateProgress();
  initDesignAreas();
  initKeyboardNav();


  // Initialise photo grid with 4 default slots
  for (let i = 0; i < 4; i++) addPhotoSlot();


  // ── AUTO SESSION RESTORE ──
  // If the user is already logged in (came from dashboard), skip login overlay
  (async function restoreSession() {
    try {
      const { data: { session } } = await _supabase.auth.getSession();
      if (!session) return; // no session — show login overlay as normal


      authToken = session.access_token;
      currentUser = session.user;
      currentUserEmail = session.user.email;


      // Fetch profile
      const { data: profiles } = await _supabase
        .from('profiles')
        .select('role, full_name')
        .eq('id', currentUser.id);


      currentUserRole = profiles?.[0]?.role || 'inspector';
      const fullName  = profiles?.[0]?.full_name || currentUserEmail.split('@')[0];


      HEADERS['Authorization'] = 'Bearer ' + authToken;
      onLoginSuccess(fullName);


      // ── LOAD INSPECTION FROM URL PARAM ──
      const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
      const loadId = params.get('load');
      if (loadId) {
        setTimeout(() => loadInspection(loadId), 400);
      }


    } catch(e) {
      console.warn('[SRC] Session restore failed:', e.message);
    }
  })();


  // Phase 3 — login screen handles connection; just show connecting state
  setDbStatus('saving', 'Sign in to connect');
</script>


<script>
// ── NARRATIVE REPORT GENERATOR ──
// Uses Anthropic API to generate a professional written narrative inspection report




function generateNarrativeText(d,g,ratings,pills,scoreC,scoreP,scoreS,scoreO,insuredName,inspId,inspDate,city,province,occupancy,inspName,riskQuality,uwRec,execSummary,yearBuilt,stories,totalArea,constructClass,extWall,roofType,roofCovering,roofYear,electrical,heating,constNotes,occupancyDesc,hazardNotes,sprinklerCoverage,sprinklerType,sprinklerCond,fireAlarm,extPresent,fusDistance,fusDeptType,fusGrade,security,protNotes,northExp,southExp,eastExp,westExp,expRating,floodZone,earthquake,expNotes,totalLosses,totalIncurred,primaryCause,lossComments,safetyText,recText) {
  function fmt(v) { return (v && v !== '\u2014') ? v : null; }
  var loc = city && province ? city + ', ' + province : (city || province || 'the subject location');
  var recItems = d.rec_items || [];
  var highRecs = recItems.filter(function(r){return r.priority==='High';});
  var medRecs  = recItems.filter(function(r){return r.priority==='Medium';});
  var NL = '\n\n';


  var s1 = '**1. Executive Summary**' + NL;
  s1 += 'This report presents the findings of a commercial property risk inspection conducted on ' + (fmt(inspDate)||'the inspection date') + ' at the premises of ' + insuredName + ', located at ' + loc + '. ';
  s1 += 'The property is occupied as ' + (fmt(occupancy)||'a commercial property') + '. ';
  s1 += 'The inspection was performed by ' + (fmt(inspName)||'the assigned inspector') + ' of Sanket Risk Consultants, covering all COPE elements, safety and compliance, loss history, and site-specific risk factors.' + NL;
  s1 += 'Based on the findings of this inspection, the overall risk quality is assessed as **' + (fmt(riskQuality)||'Standard') + '**, with an overall score of ' + (scoreO||'\u2014') + ' (Construction: ' + (scoreC||'\u2014') + ', Protection: ' + (scoreP||'\u2014') + ', Safety: ' + (scoreS||'\u2014') + '). ';
  if (recItems.length > 0) { s1 += 'A total of ' + recItems.length + ' recommendation' + (recItems.length>1?'s were':' was') + ' identified during this inspection'; if (highRecs.length) s1 += ', including ' + highRecs.length + ' high-priority item' + (highRecs.length>1?'s':''); if (medRecs.length) s1 += (highRecs.length?' and ':', including ') + medRecs.length + ' medium-priority item' + (medRecs.length>1?'s':''); s1 += '. '; }
  s1 += 'The underwriting recommendation is to **' + (fmt(uwRec)||'review') + '**.' + NL;
  if (fmt(execSummary)) { s1 += execSummary + NL; }


  var s2 = '**2. Property & Construction**' + NL;
  s2 += 'The subject property ';
  if (fmt(yearBuilt)) s2 += 'was constructed in ' + yearBuilt;
  if (fmt(stories)) s2 += (fmt(yearBuilt)?' and comprises ':'comprises ') + stories + ' stor' + (stories==='1'?'ey':'eys');
  if (fmt(totalArea)) s2 += ' with a total building area of approximately ' + parseInt(totalArea).toLocaleString() + ' square feet';
  s2 += '. ';
  if (fmt(constructClass)) {
    s2 += 'The ISO Construction Classification is ' + constructClass + '. ';
  }
  if (fmt(extWall)) {
    var wallParts = extWall.split(',');
    s2 += 'Exterior wall construction consists of ' + wallParts.map(function(p){return p.trim().toLowerCase();}).join(', ') + '. ';
  }
  if (fmt(constNotes)) s2 += constNotes + ' ';
  s2 += NL;
  s2 += 'The roof ';
  if (fmt(roofType)) s2 += 'is of ' + roofType.toLowerCase() + ' design';
  if (fmt(roofCovering)) s2 += (fmt(roofType)?' with ':'features ') + roofCovering.toLowerCase() + ' covering';
  if (fmt(roofYear)) s2 += ', last replaced in ' + roofYear;
  s2 += '. ';
  if (fmt(electrical)) s2 += 'Electrical service is provided via ' + electrical.toLowerCase() + ' panels. ';
  if (fmt(heating)) s2 += 'The heating system consists of ' + heating.toLowerCase() + '. ';
  s2 += NL;


  var s3 = '**3. Occupancy & Operations**' + NL;
  if (fmt(occupancyDesc)) { s3 += occupancyDesc + NL; } else { s3 += 'The premises are occupied as ' + (fmt(occupancy)||'a commercial property') + '. No description of operations was recorded.' + NL; }


  // Collect active hazard processes
  var hazGroup = document.getElementById('haz-processes');
  var activeHazards = [];
  if (hazGroup) {
    hazGroup.querySelectorAll('.check-btn.selected').forEach(function(btn) {
      if (btn.textContent.trim() !== 'None') activeHazards.push(btn.textContent.trim());
    });
  }


  if (activeHazards.length > 0) {
    s3 += 'The following hazardous operations or materials were identified at the time of inspection: ' + activeHazards.join(', ') + '. ' + NL;


    // Add detail for each active panel
    var hazDetails = [
      { id: 'haz-detail-cooking',  name: 'Cooking / Open Flame',
        fields: [['Equipment', 'haz-cooking-equipment'], ['Hood/Suppression', 'haz-cooking-suppression'], ['Hood Cleaning', 'haz-cooking-hood-cleaning']], notes: 'haz-cooking-notes' },
      { id: 'haz-detail-welding',  name: 'Welding / Cutting',
        fields: [['Welding Type', 'haz-welding-type'], ['Hot Work Permit', 'haz-welding-permit'], ['Designated Area', 'haz-welding-area'], ['Fire Watch', 'haz-welding-fire-watch']], notes: 'haz-welding-notes' },
      { id: 'haz-detail-spray',    name: 'Spray Painting / Coating',
        fields: [['Spray Booth', 'haz-spray-booth'], ['Booth Condition', 'haz-spray-booth-condition'], ['Flammable Coatings', 'haz-spray-flammable']], notes: 'haz-spray-notes' },
      { id: 'haz-detail-chemical', name: 'Chemical Mixing',
        fields: [['Chemical Type', 'haz-chem-type'], ['SDS Available', 'haz-chem-sds'], ['Storage Method', 'haz-chem-storage'], ['Secondary Containment', 'haz-chem-containment']], notes: 'haz-chem-notes' },
      { id: 'haz-detail-wooddust', name: 'Woodworking / Dust',
        fields: [['Dust Collection', 'haz-wood-dust-collection'], ['Accumulation Level', 'haz-wood-accumulation'], ['Finishing Operations', 'haz-wood-finishing']], notes: 'haz-wood-notes' },
      { id: 'haz-detail-compgas',  name: 'Compressed Gas',
        fields: [['Gas Types', 'haz-gas-type'], ['Cylinder Quantity', 'haz-gas-quantity'], ['Secured', 'haz-gas-secured'], ['Fuel/Oxidizer Separation', 'haz-gas-separation']], notes: 'haz-gas-notes' },
      { id: 'haz-detail-flamliq',  name: 'Flammable Liquid Storage',
        fields: [['Storage Level', 'flammable-storage'], ['Classification', 'haz-flam-class'], ['Approved Cabinet/Room', 'haz-flam-cabinet'], ['Bonding/Grounding', 'haz-flam-bonding']], notes: 'haz-flam-notes' },
      { id: 'haz-detail-cryogen',  name: 'Cryogenics',
        fields: [['Material Type', 'haz-cryo-type'], ['Vessel Type', 'haz-cryo-vessel'], ['O2 Deficiency Monitor', 'haz-cryo-monitor'], ['Ventilation', 'haz-cryo-ventilation']], notes: 'haz-cryo-notes' },
      { id: 'haz-detail-printing', name: 'Printing / Ink',
        fields: [['Operation Type', 'haz-print-type'], ['Ink/Solvent Type', 'haz-print-solvent'], ['Storage Volume', 'haz-print-volume'], ['Ventilation', 'haz-print-ventilation']], notes: 'haz-print-notes' },
    ];


    hazDetails.forEach(function(h) {
      var panel = document.getElementById(h.id);
      if (!panel || panel.style.display === 'none') return;
      var details = [];
      h.fields.forEach(function(f) {
        var el = document.getElementById(f[1]);
        var v = el ? el.value : '';
        if (v && v !== '—') details.push(f[0] + ': ' + v);
      });
      var notesEl = document.getElementById(h.notes);
      var notes = notesEl ? notesEl.value : '';
      if (details.length || notes) {
        s3 += h.name + ' — ';
        if (details.length) s3 += details.join('; ') + '. ';
        if (notes) s3 += notes + ' ';
        s3 += NL;
      }
    });
  } else if (fmt(hazardNotes) && hazardNotes !== 'None') {
    s3 += 'Hazard observations: ' + hazardNotes + NL;
  } else {
    s3 += 'No unusual hazardous operations or materials were identified at the time of inspection.' + NL;
  }
  if (fmt(hazardNotes) && activeHazards.length > 0) s3 += 'Additional hazard notes: ' + hazardNotes + NL;


  var s4 = '**4. Fire Protection & Life Safety**' + NL;
  var hasSpk = fmt(sprinklerCoverage) && sprinklerCoverage.toLowerCase().indexOf('none')===-1 && sprinklerCoverage.toLowerCase().indexOf('no') !== 0;
  if (hasSpk) { s4 += 'The building is equipped with an automatic sprinkler system providing ' + sprinklerCoverage.toLowerCase() + ' coverage'; if (fmt(sprinklerType)) s4 += ' of the ' + sprinklerType.toLowerCase() + ' type'; if (fmt(sprinklerCond)) s4 += '. System condition was noted as ' + sprinklerCond.toLowerCase(); s4 += '. '; } else { s4 += 'The building is not equipped with an automatic sprinkler system. '; }
  if (fmt(fireAlarm)) s4 += 'Fire alarm protection consists of a ' + fireAlarm.toLowerCase() + ' system. ';
  if (fmt(extPresent)) s4 += 'Portable fire extinguisher coverage is ' + extPresent.toLowerCase() + '. ';
  s4 += NL;
  s4 += 'Public fire protection is provided by ';
  if (fmt(fusDeptType)) s4 += 'a ' + fusDeptType.toLowerCase() + ' fire department';
  if (fmt(fusDistance)) s4 += ' located approximately ' + fusDistance + ' km from the premises';
  if (fmt(fusGrade)) s4 += ', with a FUS fire hall grade of ' + fusGrade;
  s4 += '. ';
  if (fmt(security)) s4 += 'Security measures in place include ' + security.toLowerCase() + '. ';
  s4 += NL;


  var s5 = '**5. Safety & Compliance**' + NL;
  var safetyList = [['Written Safety Program / Policy','safety-notes-written-safety-program-policy-text'],['Employee Safety Training Records','safety-notes-employee-safety-training-records-text'],['General Housekeeping','safety-notes-general-housekeeping-text'],['Slip / Trip / Fall Prevention','safety-notes-slip-trip-fall-prevention-text'],['Egress / Emergency Exits','safety-notes-egress-emergency-exits-text'],['Emergency Action Plan (EAP)','safety-notes-emergency-action-plan-eap-text'],['PPE \u2014 Availability & Use','safety-notes-ppe-availability-and-use-text'],['Equipment Maintenance Program','safety-notes-equipment-maintenance-program-text']];
  var totalR=0,cntR=0;
  safetyList.forEach(function(it){var r=ratings[it[0]];if(r&&'12345'.indexOf(String(r))!==-1){totalR+=parseInt(r);cntR++;}});
  var avgS = cntR>0?(totalR/cntR).toFixed(1):null;
  s5 += 'A comprehensive safety and compliance assessment was conducted covering eight key categories. ';
  if (avgS) s5 += 'The average safety rating across all categories was ' + avgS + ' out of 5. ';
  s5 += NL;
  safetyList.forEach(function(it){var el=document.getElementById(it[1]);var note=el?el.value.trim():'';if(note) s5+=it[0]+': '+note+NL;});


  var s6 = '**6. Exposure Analysis**' + NL;
  var exps=[];
  if(fmt(northExp))exps.push('to the north, '+northExp.toLowerCase());
  if(fmt(southExp))exps.push('to the south, '+southExp.toLowerCase());
  if(fmt(eastExp))exps.push('to the east, '+eastExp.toLowerCase());
  if(fmt(westExp))exps.push('to the west, '+westExp.toLowerCase());
  s6 += 'The subject property is exposed to the following neighboring risks:' + NL;
  if (exps.length) {
    exps.forEach(function(e) { s6 += '\u2022 ' + e.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + e.slice(1) + NL; });
  } else { s6 += 'No significant neighboring exposures were identified.' + NL; }
  if(fmt(expRating)) s6+='The overall exposure rating is assessed as '+expRating.toLowerCase()+'. ';
  if(fmt(floodZone)&&floodZone.toLowerCase().indexOf('no')===-1) s6+='The property is located within '+floodZone+'. ';
  if(fmt(earthquake)) s6+='Seismic exposure is classified as '+earthquake.toLowerCase()+'. ';
  s6 += NL;


  var noLoss = !fmt(totalLosses)||totalLosses==='0'||totalLosses==='\u2014';
  var s7 = '**7. Loss History**' + NL;
  if(noLoss){s7+='A review of the five-year loss history indicates no prior claims or losses on record for this risk. This is a positive underwriting indicator reflecting a well-managed property with no significant historical loss experience.'+NL;}
  else{s7+='The five-year loss history reflects '+totalLosses+' recorded loss'+(totalLosses!=='1'?'es':'')+' with a total incurred amount of $'+(fmt(totalIncurred)||'0')+'. ';if(fmt(primaryCause)&&primaryCause!=='No prior losses')s7+='The primary cause of loss is identified as '+primaryCause.toLowerCase()+'. ';if(fmt(lossComments)&&lossComments!=='N/A')s7+=lossComments+' ';s7+=NL;}


  var s8 = '**8. Recommendations & Requirements**' + NL;
  if(recItems.length===0){s8+='No recommendations or requirements were identified during this inspection. The property is maintained in satisfactory condition with no immediate corrective actions required.'+NL;}
  else{s8+='The following recommendations and requirements were identified during this inspection:'+NL;recItems.forEach(function(r){if(r.desc||r.title){s8+='**'+(r.refnum||'')+(r.refnum&&r.title?' \u2014 ':'')+(r.title||'')+'** ['+(r.priority||'Advisory')+(r.type?' '+r.type:'')+'] '+(r.desc||'')+NL;}});}


  var s9 = '**9. Underwriter Conclusions**' + NL;
  s9+='Based on the findings of this inspection, '+insuredName+' represents a '+(fmt(riskQuality)||'standard').toLowerCase()+' risk. ';
  s9+='The property is '+(noLoss?'free of prior loss history and ':'')+(recItems.length===0?'well maintained with no outstanding recommendations.':'subject to '+recItems.length+' recommendation'+(recItems.length>1?'s':'')+' as detailed above.')+' ';
  s9+='The underwriting recommendation is to **'+(fmt(uwRec)||'review')+'**';
  if(highRecs.length>0)s9+=', subject to satisfactory resolution of the '+highRecs.length+' high-priority item'+(highRecs.length>1?'s':'')+' within the specified timeframes';
  s9+='.'+NL;


  return [s1,s2,s3,s4,s5,s6,s7,s8,s9].join('');
}


async function generateNarrativeReport() {
  const d = collectFormData();
  // Helper to summarise pct_rows into readable string e.g. "Gable 90%, Flat 10%"
  function pctRowSummary(pctRows, key) {
    var rows = (pctRows || {})[key] || [];
    var filled = rows.filter(function(r) { return r.val && r.pct; });
    if (!filled.length) return '';
    return filled.map(function(r) { return r.val + ' ' + r.pct + '%'; }).join(', ');
  }
  const f = d.form_fields || {};
  const pills = d.pill_selections || {};
  const ratings = d.rating_values || {};


  const g = (id) => f[id] || '';


  // ── Build inspection data summary for the AI prompt ──
  const insuredName   = d.insured_name   || g('legal-entity')    || '—';
  const inspId        = d.inspection_id  || g('inspection-id')   || '—';
  const inspDate      = d.inspection_date|| g('inspection-date') || '—';
  const city          = d.city           || g('city')            || '—';
  const province      = d.province_state || g('province')        || '—';
  const occupancy     = d.occupancy_class|| g('occupancy-class') || '—';
  const inspName      = d.inspector_name || g('inspector-name')  || '—';
  const riskQuality   = g('risk-quality') || (pills['risk_quality_rating'] || []).join(', ')  || '—';
  const uwRec         = g('uw-recommendation') || (pills['underwriting_recommendation'] || []).join(', ') || '—';
  const execSummary   = g('executive-summary') || '';


  // Construction
  const yearBuilt     = g('year-built')   || '—';
  const stories       = g('stories-above-grade') || '—';
  const totalArea     = g('total-building-area')   || '—';
  const constructClass= (pills['iso_construction_class'] || []).join(', ') || g('iso-construction-class') || '—';
  const extWall       = (pills['exterior_wall_construction'] || []).join(', ') || g('exterior-wall-construction') || '—';
  const roofType      = pctRowSummary(d.pct_rows, 'rooftype-pct-rows') || '—';
  const roofCovering  = pctRowSummary(d.pct_rows, 'roof-pct-rows') || '—';
  const roofYear      = g('roof-year') || '—';
  const electrical    = g('electrical-panel-type') || (pills['electrical___panel_type'] || []).join(', ') || '—';
  const heating       = (pills['heating_type'] || []).join(', ') || g('heating-type') || '—';
  const constNotes    = g('construction-notes') || '';


  // Occupancy
  const occupancyDesc = g('description-operations') || '—';
  const hazardNotes   = g('hazard-notes') || '';
  const buildingValue = g('building-value-replacement-cost') || '—';


  // Protection
  const sprinklerCoverage = (pills['sprinkler_coverage'] || []).join(', ') || g('sprinkler-coverage') || '—';
  const sprinklerType     = g('sprinkler-type') || '—';
  const sprinklerCond     = g('sprinkler-condition') || '—';
  const fireAlarm         = (pills['fire_alarm_system'] || []).join(', ') || g('fire-alarm-system') || '—';
  const extPresent        = g('extinguishers-present') || '—';
  const fusDistance       = g('fus-distance-firehall') || '—';
  const fusDeptType       = g('fus-dept-type') || '—';
  const fusGrade          = g('fus-firehall-grade') || '—';
  const security          = (pills['security_measures'] || []).join(', ') || '—';
  const protNotes         = g('fus-notes') || '';


  // Exposure
  const northExp      = g('north-exposure') || '—';
  const southExp      = g('south-exposure') || '—';
  const eastExp       = g('east-exposure')  || '—';
  const westExp       = g('west-exposure')  || '—';
  const expRating     = g('exposure-rating') || '—';
  const floodZone     = g('flood-zone') || '—';
  const earthquake    = g('earthquake-zone') || g('earthquake-pga') || '—';
  const expNotes      = g('exposure-notes') || '';


  // Safety ratings
  var safetyItems = [
    ['Written Safety Program / Policy',    'safety-notes-written-safety-program-policy-text'],
    ['Employee Safety Training Records',   'safety-notes-employee-safety-training-records-text'],
    ['General Housekeeping',               'safety-notes-general-housekeeping-text'],
    ['Slip / Trip / Fall Prevention',      'safety-notes-slip-trip-fall-prevention-text'],
    ['Egress / Emergency Exits',           'safety-notes-egress-emergency-exits-text'],
    ['Emergency Action Plan (EAP)',        'safety-notes-emergency-action-plan-eap-text'],
    ['PPE — Availability & Use',           'safety-notes-ppe-availability-and-use-text'],
    ['Equipment Maintenance Program',      'safety-notes-equipment-maintenance-program-text'],
