  ];
  var safetyText = safetyItems.map(function(item) {
    var label = item[0], noteId = item[1];
    var rating = ratings[label] || '—';
    var noteEl = document.getElementById(noteId);
    var note = noteEl ? noteEl.value.trim() : (d.safety_notes && d.safety_notes[noteId.replace('-text','')] ? d.safety_notes[noteId.replace('-text','')] : '');
    return label + ': ' + rating + '/5' + (note ? ' — ' + note : '');
  }).join('\n');


  // Recommendations
  var recText = '';
  if (d.rec_items && d.rec_items.length) {
    recText = d.rec_items.map(function(r, i) {
      return (r.refnum || (i+1)) + '. [' + (r.priority||'') + '] ' + (r.title||'') + ': ' + (r.desc||'');
    }).join('\n');
  }


  // Loss history
  var totalLosses = g('total-losses') || '0';
  var totalIncurred = g('total-incurred-amount') || '0';
  var primaryCause = g('primary-cause') || 'No prior losses';
  var lossComments = g('loss-comments') || '';


  // Score tiles
  var scoreC = document.getElementById('score-construction') ? document.getElementById('score-construction').textContent : '—';
  var scoreP = document.getElementById('score-protection')   ? document.getElementById('score-protection').textContent   : '—';
  var scoreS = document.getElementById('score-safety')       ? document.getElementById('score-safety').textContent       : '—';
  var scoreO = document.getElementById('score-overall')      ? document.getElementById('score-overall').textContent      : '—';


  // ── Build AI prompt ──
  var prompt = `You are a senior commercial property inspector writing a formal narrative inspection report for an insurance underwriter. Write in professional, clear, third-person prose. Be specific and factual. Use the inspection data below.


INSPECTION DATA:
Insured: ${insuredName}
Inspection ID: ${inspId}
Date: ${inspDate}
Location: ${city}, ${province}
Occupancy: ${occupancy}
Inspector: ${inspName}
Risk Quality: ${riskQuality}
UW Recommendation: ${uwRec}


CONSTRUCTION:
Year Built: ${yearBuilt} | Stories: ${stories} | Total Area: ${totalArea} sq ft
Construction Class: ${constructClass}
Exterior Walls: ${extWall}
Roof Type: ${roofType} | Roof Covering: ${roofCovering} | Roof Last Replaced: ${roofYear}
Electrical: ${electrical} | Heating: ${heating}
Notes: ${constNotes}


OCCUPANCY:
${occupancyDesc}
Hazards: ${hazardNotes}


PROTECTION:
Sprinkler Coverage: ${sprinklerCoverage} | Type: ${sprinklerType} | Condition: ${sprinklerCond}
Fire Alarm: ${fireAlarm}
Extinguishers: ${extPresent}
FUS: ${fusDistance}km to ${fusDeptType} fire hall | Grade: ${fusGrade}
Security: ${security}
Notes: ${protNotes}


EXPOSURE:
North: ${northExp} | South: ${southExp} | East: ${eastExp} | West: ${westExp}
Overall: ${expRating} | Flood Zone: ${floodZone} | Seismic: ${earthquake}
Notes: ${expNotes}


LOSS HISTORY (5 yr):
Total Losses: ${totalLosses} | Total Incurred: $${totalIncurred}
Primary Cause: ${primaryCause}
${lossComments}


SAFETY ASSESSMENT (1-5 scale):
${safetyText}


SCORES: Construction ${scoreC} | Protection ${scoreP} | Safety ${scoreS} | Overall ${scoreO}


RECOMMENDATIONS:
${recText || 'None recorded.'}


INSPECTOR EXECUTIVE SUMMARY:
${execSummary}


---
Write a complete narrative inspection report with the following sections:
1. **Executive Summary** (2-3 paragraphs): Overall risk quality, key findings, underwriting recommendation
2. **Property & Construction** (2 paragraphs): Building description, construction quality, systems
3. **Occupancy & Operations** (1-2 paragraphs): Use of premises, occupancy hazards, operational observations
4. **Fire Protection & Life Safety** (2 paragraphs): Active and passive systems, FUS grading, extinguisher coverage
5. **Safety & Compliance** (1-2 paragraphs): Safety program quality, key observations per category
6. **Exposure Analysis** (1 paragraph): Neighboring exposures, natural hazards
7. **Loss History** (1 paragraph): Prior loss experience and trend
8. **Recommendations Summary** (concise paragraph): Key requirements and recommendations with reference numbers
9. **Underwriter Conclusions** (1 paragraph): Final risk assessment and conditions


Write in formal insurance inspection language. Be specific with measurements, dates, and observations. Do not use bullet points — write in full paragraphs only.`;


  // ── Open new tab and show loading state ──
  var w = window.open('', '_blank');
  if (!w) {
    alert('Please allow popups for this site to view the Narrative Report.');
    return;
  }


  var loadingHTML = `<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
<meta charset="UTF-8">
<title>Generating Narrative Report...</title>
<link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Playfair+Display:wght@400;600;700&family=IBM+Plex+Sans:wght@300;400;500;600&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
<style>
  body { font-family: 'IBM Plex Sans', sans-serif; background: #f8f5f0; display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center; min-height: 100vh; margin: 0; }
  .loading { text-align: center; color: #0d1b2a; }
  .spinner { width: 48px; height: 48px; border: 4px solid #e8d5a3; border-top-color: #0d1b2a; border-radius: 50%; animation: spin 1s linear infinite; margin: 0 auto 20px; }
  @keyframes spin { to { transform: rotate(360deg); } }
  h2 { font-family: 'Playfair Display', serif; font-size: 22px; margin-bottom: 8px; }
  p { color: #4a6580; font-size: 14px; }
</style>
</head>
<body>
<div class="loading">
  <div class="spinner"></div>
  <h2>Generating Narrative Report</h2>
  <p>Claude AI is writing your inspection narrative for<br><strong>${insuredName}</strong>...</p>
</div>
</body>
</html>`;


  // ── Generate narrative instantly (template-based) ──
  try {
    var narrativeText = generateNarrativeText(d, g, ratings, pills, scoreC, scoreP, scoreS, scoreO,
      insuredName, inspId, inspDate, city, province, occupancy, inspName,
      riskQuality, uwRec, execSummary, yearBuilt, stories, totalArea,
      constructClass, extWall, roofType, roofCovering, roofYear,
      electrical, heating, constNotes, occupancyDesc, hazardNotes,
      sprinklerCoverage, sprinklerType, sprinklerCond, fireAlarm,
      extPresent, fusDistance, fusDeptType, fusGrade, security, protNotes,
      northExp, southExp, eastExp, westExp, expRating, floodZone, earthquake, expNotes,
      totalLosses, totalIncurred, primaryCause, lossComments, safetyText, recText);


    // ── Convert markdown to HTML ──
    function mdToHtml(text) {
      return text
        .replace(/\*\*([^*]+)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>')
        .replace(/^#{1,3}\s+(.+)$/gm, '<h3>$1</h3>')
        .replace(/^\d+\.\s+\*\*([^*]+)\*\*:?\s*/gm, '<h3>$1</h3>')
        .replace(/^\d+\.\s+\*\*([^*]+)\*\*/gm, '<h3>$1</h3>')
        .replace(/\n\n/g, '</p><p>')
        .replace(/^(.)/m, '<p>$1')
        + '</p>';
    }


    var narrativeHTML = mdToHtml(narrativeText);


    // ── Build final report page ──
    var reportPage = `<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
<meta charset="UTF-8">
<meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
<title>Narrative Report — ${insuredName}</title>
<link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Playfair+Display:wght@400;600;700&family=IBM+Plex+Sans:wght@300;400;500;600&family=IBM+Plex+Mono:wght@400;500&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
<style>
  :root { --navy:#0d1b2a; --gold:#c9a84c; --gold-light:#e8d5a3; --cream:#f8f5f0; --slate:#4a6580; --border:#ddd8d0; }
  * { margin:0; padding:0; box-sizing:border-box; }
  body { font-family:'IBM Plex Sans',sans-serif; font-size:11pt; color:#1a2433; background:white; line-height:1.7; }


  .toolbar { position:fixed; top:0; left:0; right:0; height:52px; background:var(--navy); display:flex; align-items:center; justify-content:space-between; padding:0 32px; z-index:1000; }
  .toolbar-left { color:white; font-size:13px; font-family:'Playfair Display',serif; }
  .toolbar-left span { color:var(--gold); }
  .btn-print { background:var(--gold); color:var(--navy); border:none; padding:8px 22px; border-radius:6px; font-size:12px; font-weight:700; cursor:pointer; font-family:inherit; }
  .btn-close { background:rgba(255,255,255,0.1); color:white; border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.2); padding:8px 18px; border-radius:6px; font-size:12px; cursor:pointer; font-family:inherit; }


  .report-wrap { padding-top:72px; max-width:820px; margin:0 auto; padding-bottom:80px; padding-left:40px; padding-right:40px; }


  .cover-band { background:var(--navy); color:white; padding:36px 40px; border-radius:10px; margin-bottom:36px; }
  .cover-band .tag { font-size:8pt; letter-spacing:.2em; text-transform:uppercase; color:var(--gold-light); margin-bottom:6px; }
  .cover-band h1 { font-family:'Playfair Display',serif; font-size:22pt; color:white; margin-bottom:4px; }
  .cover-band .sub { font-size:10pt; color:#7a9ab5; margin-bottom:20px; }
  .meta-grid { display:grid; grid-template-columns:repeat(3,1fr); gap:12px 24px; }
  .meta-item label { font-size:7.5pt; color:#7a9ab5; text-transform:uppercase; letter-spacing:.06em; display:block; margin-bottom:2px; }
  .meta-item span { font-size:10pt; color:white; font-weight:600; }


  .ai-badge { display:inline-flex; align-items:center; gap:6px; background:rgba(201,168,76,0.15); border:1px solid var(--gold); border-radius:20px; padding:4px 12px; font-size:9pt; color:var(--gold-light); margin-bottom:24px; }


  .section { margin-bottom:32px; }
  .section h3 { font-family:'Playfair Display',serif; font-size:13pt; color:var(--navy); padding-bottom:8px; border-bottom:2px solid var(--gold); margin-bottom:14px; }
  .section p { margin-bottom:12px; font-size:11pt; line-height:1.75; color:#1a2433; }
  .section strong { color:var(--navy); }


  .disclaimer { margin-top:40px; padding:14px 18px; background:#f8f5f0; border-left:3px solid var(--gold); border-radius:0 6px 6px 0; font-size:8.5pt; color:var(--slate); line-height:1.6; }


  @media print {
    .toolbar { display:none; }
    .report-wrap { padding-top:20px; max-width:100%; }
    @page { margin:1.5cm; size:letter; }
    .section { page-break-inside:avoid; }
  }
</style>
</head>
<body>


<div class="toolbar no-print">
  <div class="toolbar-left"><span>S</span> Sanket Risk Consultants — Narrative Inspection Report</div>
  <div style="display:flex;gap:10px;">
    <button class="btn-print" onclick="window.print()">🖨 Print / Save PDF</button>
    <button class="btn-close" onclick="window.close()">✕ Close</button>
  </div>
</div>


<div class="report-wrap">
  <div class="cover-band">
    <div class="tag">N A R R A T I V E &nbsp; I N S P E C T I O N &nbsp; R E P O R T</div>
    <h1>${insuredName}</h1>
    <div class="sub">${city}, ${province} &nbsp;·&nbsp; ${occupancy}</div>
    <div class="meta-grid">
      <div class="meta-item"><label>Inspection ID</label><span>${inspId}</span></div>
      <div class="meta-item"><label>Date of Inspection</label><span>${inspDate}</span></div>
      <div class="meta-item"><label>Inspector</label><span>${inspName}</span></div>
      <div class="meta-item"><label>Risk Quality</label><span style="color:var(--gold);">${riskQuality}</span></div>
      <div class="meta-item"><label>UW Recommendation</label><span style="color:var(--gold);">${uwRec}</span></div>
      <div class="meta-item"><label>Overall Score</label><span>${scoreO !== '—' ? scoreO + ' / 5' : '—'}</span></div>
    </div>
    <div style="margin-top:16px;padding-top:14px;border-top:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.15);display:flex;gap:24px;flex-wrap:wrap;">
      <div style="font-size:8pt;color:#7a9ab5;"><span style="color:var(--gold-light);font-weight:600;">Construction</span>&nbsp; ${scoreC !== '—' ? scoreC + '/5' : '—'}</div>
      <div style="font-size:8pt;color:#7a9ab5;"><span style="color:var(--gold-light);font-weight:600;">Protection</span>&nbsp; ${scoreP !== '—' ? scoreP + '/5' : '—'}</div>
      <div style="font-size:8pt;color:#7a9ab5;"><span style="color:var(--gold-light);font-weight:600;">Safety</span>&nbsp; ${scoreS !== '—' ? scoreS + '/5' : '—'}</div>
    </div>
  </div>


  <div class="ai-badge">✦ Sanket Risk Consultants &nbsp;·&nbsp; Narrative Report &nbsp;·&nbsp; Review before finalising</div>


  <div class="section narrative-content">
    ${narrativeHTML}
  </div>


  <div class="disclaimer">
    <strong>Report Disclaimer:</strong> This narrative was generated by the SanketRisk Inspector platform based on structured inspection data entered by the inspector. It is intended as a drafting aid only. The inspector and underwriter are responsible for verifying all factual claims, correcting any inaccuracies, and ensuring the report meets applicable professional and regulatory standards before use.
  </div>
</div>


</body>
</html>`;


    w.document.open();
    w.document.write(reportPage);
    w.document.close();


  } catch(err) {
    w.document.open();
    w.document.write('<html><body style="font-family:sans-serif;padding:40px;"><h2>Error generating narrative</h2><p>' + err.message + '</p></body></html>');
    w.document.close();
    console.error('Narrative error:', err);
  }
}

<script>
// This will be injected into index.html
// Formal Report Generator — opens in new tab


function generateFormalReport() {
  try {
  const d = collectFormData();
  const f = d.form_fields || {};
  const pills = d.pill_selections || {};
  const ratings = d.rating_values || {};
  const pct = d.pct_rows || {};
  const fin = d.finish_rows || {};


  const g = (id) => f[id] || '';
  const fmt = (v) => v || '—';
  // Get selected option text (for selects that display text, not value)
  const selText = (id) => {
    var el = document.getElementById(id);
    if (!el) return f[id] || '—';
    if (el.tagName === 'SELECT' && el.selectedIndex >= 0) {
      var opt = el.options[el.selectedIndex];
      return (opt && opt.text && opt.text !== '— Select —') ? opt.text : (f[id] || '—');
    }
    return f[id] || '—';
  };


  // ── Helpers ──
  function pctTable(containerId) {
    const rows = pct[containerId] || [];
    const filled = rows.filter(r => r.val && r.pct);
    if (!filled.length) return '<span class="val-empty">—</span>';
    return filled.map(r => `<span class="pct-item"><span class="pct-label">${r.val}</span><span class="pct-num">${r.pct}%</span></span>`).join('');
  }


  function finTable(containerId) {
    const rows = fin[containerId] || [];
    const filled = rows.filter(r => r.val);
    if (!filled.length) return '<span class="val-empty">—</span>';
    return filled.map(r => `<span class="pct-item"><span class="pct-label">${r.val}${r.note ? ' — ' + r.note : ''}</span><span class="pct-num">${r.pct || ''}${r.pct ? '%' : ''}</span></span>`).join('');
  }


  function pillVal(key) {
    const arr = pills[key] || [];
    return arr.length ? arr.join(', ') : '—';
  }


  function ratingVal(label) {
    return ratings[label] || '—';
  }


  function val(id) {
    const v = f[id];
    return v && v !== '' ? v : '—';
  }


  function secHeader(icon, title, tag) {
    return `<div class="sec-header">
      <div class="sec-header-left">
        <span class="sec-icon">${icon}</span>
        <span class="sec-title">${title}</span>
      </div>
      <span class="sec-tag">${tag}</span>
    </div>`;
  }


  function field2(label, value) {
    return `<div class="field-block">
      <div class="field-label">${label}</div>
      <div class="field-value">${value || '—'}</div>
    </div>`;
  }


  function fieldFull(label, value) {
    return `<div class="field-block field-full">
      <div class="field-label">${label}</div>
      <div class="field-value">${value || '—'}</div>
    </div>`;
  }


  // ── Recommendations — read from DOM (current session data) ──
  const recItems = [];
  // First try from saved data (for loaded inspections)
  if (d.rec_items && d.rec_items.length) {
    d.rec_items.forEach(function(r) {
      if (r.desc) recItems.push(r);
    });
  }
  // If no saved data, read directly from DOM
  if (!recItems.length) {
  const recList = document.getElementById('rec-list');
  if (recList) {
    recList.querySelectorAll('.rec-item').forEach(function(item, idx) {
      // Priority: find selected radio button
      var priorityBtn = item.querySelector('.radio-btn.selected[data-level]');
      var levelMap = { high: 'High', med: 'Medium', low: 'Low' };
      var priority = priorityBtn ? (levelMap[priorityBtn.getAttribute('data-level')] || '') : '';


      // Type: first select
      var selects = item.querySelectorAll('select');
      var type = selects[0] ? selects[0].value : '';


      // Description: first textarea
      var textareas = item.querySelectorAll('textarea');
      var desc = textareas[0] ? textareas[0].value.trim() : '';


      // Section: second select
      var section = selects[1] ? selects[1].value : '';


      // Consequence: fourth select (index 3)
      var consequence = selects[3] ? selects[3].value : '';


      // Notes: second textarea (rec-notes-field)
      var notesEl = item.querySelector('.rec-notes-field') || textareas[1];
      var notes = notesEl ? notesEl.value.trim() : '';
      var titleEl = item.querySelector('.rec-title-field');
      var title = titleEl ? titleEl.value.trim() : '';
      var refEl = item.querySelector('.rec-ref-field');
      var refnum = refEl ? refEl.value.trim() : '';


      if (desc) {
        recItems.push({
          num: idx + 1,
          title: title,
          refnum: refnum,
          desc: desc,
          priority: priority,
          type: type,
          section: section,
          notes: notes,
          consequence: consequence
        });
      }
    });
  }
  } // end DOM fallback


  // Keep recommendations in original entry order to preserve inspector numbering
  // Priority is shown via colour badges — no need to re-sort
  // Auto-fill refnum only for items that have no reference number
  recItems.forEach(function(r, i) {
    if (!r.refnum) {
      r.refnum = yearPart + '-' + monPart + '-' + String(i + 1).padStart(3, '0');
    }
  });


  function priorityBadge(p) {
    const cls = p === 'High' ? 'badge-high' : p === 'Medium' ? 'badge-med' : p === 'Low' ? 'badge-low' : 'badge-default';
    return `<span class="priority-badge ${cls}">${p || '—'}</span>`;
  }


  function typeBadge(t) {
    const cls = t === 'Requirement' ? 'badge-req' : 'badge-rec';
    return `<span class="type-badge ${cls}">${t || '—'}</span>`;
  }


  // ── Risk Quality ──
  const rqRaw = g('risk-quality') || pillVal('risk_quality_rating') || d.risk_quality || '';
  const uwRec = g('uw-recommendation') || d.uw_recommendation || '';
  const sprGrade = g('spk-final-grade') || '';
  const sprScore = g('spk-score') || '';
  const sprGradeLabel = sprGrade ? 'Grade ' + sprGrade + (sprScore ? ' (Score: ' + sprScore + '/100)' : '') : '—';


  // ── Inspection details ──
  const inspId = d.inspection_id || g('inspection-id') || '—';
  const acctNum = d.account_number || g('account-number') || '—';
  const policyNum = d.policy_number || g('policy-number') || '—';
  const inspDate = d.inspection_date || g('inspection-date') || '—';
  const insuredName = d.insured_name || g('legal-entity') || '—';
  const city = d.city || g('city') || '—';
  const province = d.province_state || g('province') || '—';
  const occupancy = d.occupancy_class || g('occupancy-class') || '—';
  const inspName = d.inspector_name || g('inspector-name') || '—';
  const inspOrg = g('inspector-org') || 'Sanket Risk Consultants';


  // Auto-fill refnum if blank: YYYY-MM-NNN from inspection date
  var yearPart = (inspDate && inspDate !== '—') ? inspDate.substring(0, 4) : new Date().getFullYear().toString();
  var monPart = (inspDate && inspDate !== '—') ? inspDate.substring(5, 7) : String(new Date().getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0');


  // Photo for cover
  const photo1 = document.getElementById('photo-1-img');
  const coverPhotoSrc = (photo1 && photo1.classList.contains('loaded') && photo1.src) ? photo1.src : '';


  // Collect ALL photo data now (before window.open) so we don't need window.opener
  const allPhotos = [];
  let photoIdx = 1;
  while (photoIdx <= 20) {
    const img = document.getElementById('photo-' + photoIdx + '-img');
    if (!img && photoIdx > 10) break;
    if (img && img.classList.contains('loaded') && img.src) {
      const captionEl = document.getElementById('photo-' + photoIdx + '-caption');
      const categoryEl = document.getElementById('photo-' + photoIdx + '-category');
      allPhotos.push({
        num: photoIdx,
        src: img.src,
        caption: captionEl ? captionEl.value : '',
        category: categoryEl ? categoryEl.value : ''
      });
    }
    photoIdx++;
  }


  // Score tiles
  var _sc = document.getElementById('score-construction');
  var _sp = document.getElementById('score-protection');
  var _ss = document.getElementById('score-safety');
  var _so = document.getElementById('score-overall');
  const scoreC = (_sc ? _sc.textContent : '') || '—';
  const scoreP = (_sp ? _sp.textContent : '') || '—';
  const scoreS = (_ss ? _ss.textContent : '') || '—';
  const scoreO = (_so ? _so.textContent : '') || '—';


  // Supplements active
  const activeSuppNames = {
    'restaurant': 'Restaurant / Food Service',
    'woodworking': 'Woodworking / Lumber',
    'warehouse': 'Warehouse / Distribution',
    'autoservice': 'Auto Service / Repair',
    'sprinkler': 'Sprinkler Grading',
    'apartments': 'Apartments / Condominiums',
  };
  const activeSupps = (d.active_supplements || []).map(s => activeSuppNames[s] || s);
  const activeGL = (d.active_gl_modules || []);


  // Generate TOC entries
  const tocSections = [
    { num: 1, title: 'Assignment Overview', id: 'sec-intro' },
    { num: 2, title: 'Insured & Property Information', id: 'sec-insured' },
    { num: 3, title: 'Construction (COPE — C)', id: 'sec-construction' },
    { num: 4, title: 'Occupancy (COPE — O)', id: 'sec-occupancy' },
    { num: 5, title: 'Protection (COPE — P)', id: 'sec-protection' },
    { num: 6, title: 'Exposure (COPE — E)', id: 'sec-exposure' },
    { num: 7, title: 'Loss History', id: 'sec-loss' },
    { num: 8, title: 'Safety & Compliance', id: 'sec-safety' },
    { num: 9, title: 'Recommendations & Requirements', id: 'sec-recommendations' },
    { num: 10, title: 'Underwriter Summary', id: 'sec-summary' },
  ];
  let tocNum = 11;
  const suppDisplayNames = {
    'restaurant': 'Restaurant / Food Service',
    'woodworking': 'Woodworking / Lumber',
    'warehouse': 'Warehouse / Distribution',
    'autoservice': 'Auto Service / Repair',
    'sprinkler': 'Sprinkler Grading',
    'apartments': 'Apartments / Condominiums',
  };
  if ((d.active_supplements || []).length) {
    (d.active_supplements || []).forEach(s => {
      var name = suppDisplayNames[s] || s;
      tocSections.push({ num: tocNum++, title: 'Supplement: ' + name, id: 'sec-supp-' + s });
    });
  }
  tocSections.push({ num: tocNum++, title: 'Photo Documentation', id: 'sec-photos' });




  // ── Build supplement sections for active supplements ──
  function buildSuppSection(suppId) {
    const g = (id) => f[id] || '';
    const fmt = (v) => v || '—';
    
    if (suppId === 'restaurant') {
      return secHeader('🍳', 'Restaurant / Food Service Supplement', 'SUPP — RESTAURANT') +
        '<div class="sec-body">' +
        '<div class="sub-heading">Cooking Equipment</div>' +
        '<div class="field-grid">' +
        field2('Type of Cooking Operations', fmt(g('type-of-cooking-operations'))) +
        field2('Number of Deep Fryers', fmt(g('number-of-deep-fryers'))) +
        field2('Char-Broiler Present?', fmt(g('char-broiler-present'))) +
        field2('Solid Fuel Cooking?', fmt(g('solid-fuel-cooking'))) +
        field2('Total Cooking BTU Load', fmt(g('total-cooking-btu-load'))) +
        field2('Gas Shutoff — Accessible?', fmt(g('gas-shutoff-accessible'))) +
        '</div>' +
        '<div class="sub-heading">Hood &amp; Suppression System</div>' +
        '<div class="field-grid">' +
        field2('Type I Hood Present?', fmt(g('type-i-hood-present'))) +
        field2('Hood Suppression System', fmt(g('hood-suppression-system'))) +
        field2('Last Hood Suppression Service', fmt(g('last-hood-suppression-service'))) +
        field2('Service Frequency', fmt(g('service-frequency'))) +
        field2('Hood Cleaning Frequency', fmt(g('hood-cleaning-frequency'))) +
        field2('Grease Accumulation Observed?', fmt(g('grease-accumulation-observed'))) +
        field2('Grease Filter Condition', fmt(g('grease-filter-condition'))) +
        field2('Grease Trap / Interceptor', fmt(g('grease-trap-interceptor'))) +
        '</div>' +
        fieldFull('Hood / Suppression Notes', fmt(g('hood-suppression-notes'))) +
        '<div class="sub-heading">Refrigeration, Storage &amp; Operations</div>' +
        '<div class="field-grid">' +
        field2('Walk-In Cooler / Freezer?', fmt(g('walk-in-cooler-freezer'))) +
        field2('Walk-In Condition', fmt(g('walk-in-condition'))) +
        field2('Seating Capacity', fmt(g('seating-capacity'))) +
        field2('Liquor / Alcohol Service?', fmt(g('liquor-alcohol-service'))) +
        field2('Last Health Inspection', fmt(g('last-health-inspection'))) +
        field2('Health Inspection Result', fmt(g('health-inspection-result'))) +
        '</div>' +
        fieldFull('Restaurant Operations Notes', fmt(g('restaurant-operations-notes'))) +
        '</div>';
    }
    
    if (suppId === 'woodworking') {
      return secHeader('🪚', 'Woodworking / Lumber Supplement', 'SUPP — WOODWORKING') +
        '<div class="sec-body">' +
        '<div class="sub-heading">Operations &amp; Machinery</div>' +
        '<div class="field-grid">' +
        field2('Type of Woodworking Operations', fmt(g('type-of-woodworking-operations'))) +
        field2('Hours of Operation', fmt(g('hours-of-operation-1'))) +
        field2('Major Machinery Present', fmt(g('major-machinery-present-table-saw-band-saw-planer'))) +
        field2('Lockout / Tagout Program?', fmt(g('lockout-tagout-program'))) +
        '</div>' +
        '<div class="sub-heading">Dust Collection &amp; Combustible Dust</div>' +
        '<div class="field-grid">' +
        field2('Dust Collection System', fmt(g('dust-collection-system'))) +
        field2('Dust Collector Location', fmt(g('dust-collector-location'))) +
        field2('Dust Collector — Spark Arrestor?', fmt(g('dust-collector-spark-arrestor'))) +
        field2('Dust Collector — Last Cleaned', fmt(g('dust-collector-last-cleaned'))) +
        field2('Sawdust / Wood Dust Accumulation', fmt(g('sawdust-wood-dust-accumulation'))) +

  // ── NAVIGATION ──
  function showSection(id, el) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.section-panel').forEach(p => {
      p.classList.remove('active');
    });
    document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item, .supp-nav-item').forEach(n => n.classList.remove('active'));
    const panel = document.getElementById('section-' + id);
    if (panel) {
      panel.classList.add('active');
    }
    if (el) el.classList.add('active');
    updateProgress();
    window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
    setTimeout(() => {
      const first = panel && panel.querySelector('input:not([type=hidden]), select, textarea, .radio-btn[tabindex], .check-btn[tabindex], button:not(.btn-remove-area)');
      if (first) first.focus();
    }, 50);
  }
  // ── RADIO BUTTONS ──
  function selectRadio(el, groupId) {
    const group = document.getElementById(groupId) || el.closest('.radio-group');
    if (group) group.querySelectorAll('.radio-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('selected'));
    el.classList.add('selected');
  }
  // ── CHECKBOXES ──
  function toggleCheck(el) {
    el.classList.toggle('selected');
  }
  function toggleHazDetail(key, btn) {
    const panel = document.getElementById('haz-detail-' + key);
    if (!panel) return;
    const isSelected = btn.classList.contains('selected');
    panel.style.display = isSelected ? 'block' : 'none';
  }

  function showNFPAGuide(val) {
    const guide = document.getElementById('nfpa-guide');
    const body  = document.getElementById('nfpa-guide-body');
    if (!val || !NFPA_GUIDE[val]) { guide.style.display = 'none'; return; }
    const g = NFPA_GUIDE[val];
    body.innerHTML =
      '<div style="margin-bottom:8px;">' + g.desc + '</div>' +
      '<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:8px;margin-top:8px;">' +
        '<div style="background:#fff;border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:6px;padding:8px 10px;">' +
          '<div style="font-size:10px;font-weight:700;color:var(--slate);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.06em;margin-bottom:4px;">Typical Occupancies</div>' +
          '<div style="color:var(--navy);">' + g.examples + '</div>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div style="background:#fff;border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:6px;padding:8px 10px;">' +
          '<div style="font-size:10px;font-weight:700;color:var(--slate);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.06em;margin-bottom:4px;">Fire Protection Considerations</div>' +
          '<div style="color:var(--navy);">' + g.controls + '</div>' +
        '</div>' +
      '</div>' +
      '<div style="margin-top:8px;background:#fff;border-left:3px solid ' + g.color + ';border-radius:0 6px 6px 0;padding:8px 12px;border:1px solid var(--border);">' +
        '<span style="font-size:10px;font-weight:700;color:var(--slate);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.06em;">UW Signal — </span>' +
        '<span style="font-weight:600;color:' + g.color + ';">' + g.uw + '</span>' +
      '</div>';
    guide.style.display = 'block';
  }
  // ── RATINGS ──
  function setRating(btn, val) {
    const row = btn.closest('.rating-btns');
    row.querySelectorAll('.rating-btn').forEach(b => {
      b.classList.remove('sel');
    });
    btn.classList.add('sel');
    updateSafetyScore();
  }
  function updateSafetyScore() {
    const rows = document.querySelectorAll('#safety-ratings .rating-btns');
    let total = 0, count = 0;
    rows.forEach(row => {
      const sel = row.querySelector('.sel');
      if (sel) { total += parseInt(sel.textContent); count++; }
    });
    if (count > 0) {
      const avg = (total/count).toFixed(1);
      document.getElementById('score-safety').textContent = avg;
      updateOverallScore();
    }
  }
  function updateOverallScore() {
    const vals = ['score-construction','score-protection','score-safety']
      .map(id => parseFloat(document.getElementById(id).textContent))
      .filter(v => !isNaN(v));
    if (vals.length) {
      document.getElementById('score-overall').textContent =
        (vals.reduce((a,b) => a+b, 0) / vals.length).toFixed(1);
    }
  }

  function setRecPriority(el, recId, level) {
    const item = document.getElementById(recId);
    if (!item) {
      // Fallback: find parent rec-item via DOM traversal
      var parent = el.closest('.rec-item');
      if (parent) parent.className = 'rec-item priority-' + level;
    } else {
      item.className = 'rec-item priority-' + level;
    }
    var group = el.closest('.radio-group');
    if (group) group.querySelectorAll('.radio-btn').forEach(function(b) { b.classList.remove('selected'); });
    el.classList.add('selected');
  }

  // ── PHOTO DOCUMENTATION ──
  let photoCount = 0;
  const PHOTO_CATEGORIES = [
    '— Category —',
    'Exterior — Front', 'Exterior — Rear/Sides', 'Exterior — Aerial',
    'Roof — Overview', 'Roof — Detail', 'Roof — Drain/Parapet',

  function makePhotoSlot(num) {
    const id = `photo-${num}`;
    const wrap = document.createElement('div');
    wrap.className = 'photo-card';
    wrap.id = `photo-card-${num}`;
    wrap.innerHTML = `
      <div class="photo-preview-wrap" onclick="triggerPhotoUpload(${num})">
        <img id="${id}-img" alt="Photo ${num}">
        <div class="photo-placeholder" id="${id}-placeholder">
          <div class="photo-placeholder-icon">📷</div>
          <div class="photo-placeholder-text">Click to add Photo ${num}</div>
        </div>
        <button class="photo-remove-btn" onclick="clearPhoto(event, ${num})" title="Remove photo">✕</button>
      </div>
      <div class="photo-meta">
        <div class="photo-num">Photo ${num}</div>
        <input type="text" id="${id}-caption" placeholder="Caption — describe what is shown" style="font-size:12px;">
        <select id="${id}-category" style="font-size:12px;margin-top:2px;">
          ${PHOTO_CATEGORIES.map(c => `<option>${c}</option>`).join('')}
        </select>
      </div>
      <input type="file" id="${id}-file" accept="image/*" style="display:none"
        onchange="handlePhotoFile(${num}, this)">`;
    return wrap;
  }
  function triggerPhotoUpload(num) {
    document.getElementById(`photo-${num}-file`).click();
  }
  function handlePhotoFile(num, input) {
    const file = input.files[0];
    if (!file) return;
    // Show preview immediately from local file
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = e => {
      const img = document.getElementById('photo-' + num + '-img');
      const placeholder = document.getElementById('photo-' + num + '-placeholder');
      img.src = e.target.result;
      img.classList.add('loaded');
      img.setAttribute('data-local', '1'); // mark as local only until uploaded
      placeholder.style.display = 'none';
    };
    reader.readAsDataURL(file);
    // Upload to Supabase Storage in background
    uploadPhotoToStorage(num, file);
  }
  async function uploadPhotoToStorage(num, file) {
    if (!currentInspectionId) {
      // No inspection saved yet — queue for upload after save
      pendingPhotoUploads[num] = file;
      return;
    }
    try {
      const ext = file.name.split('.').pop() || 'jpg';
      const path = 'inspections/' + currentInspectionId + '/photo-' + num + '.' + ext;
      const { data, error } = await _supabase.storage
        .from('inspection-photos')
        .upload(path, file, { upsert: true, contentType: file.type });
      if (error) throw error;
      // Store the storage path on the img element for saving
      const img = document.getElementById('photo-' + num + '-img');
      if (img) {
        img.setAttribute('data-storage-path', path);
        img.removeAttribute('data-local');
      }
      console.log('Photo ' + num + ' uploaded to storage: ' + path);
    } catch(e) {
      console.warn('Photo ' + num + ' storage upload failed (will retry on save):', e.message);
      pendingPhotoUploads[num] = file;
    }
  }
  var pendingPhotoUploads = {};
  async function flushPendingPhotoUploads() {
    if (!currentInspectionId) return;
    const pending = Object.entries(pendingPhotoUploads);
    for (const [num, file] of pending) {
      await uploadPhotoToStorage(parseInt(num), file);
      delete pendingPhotoUploads[num];
    }
  }
  function clearPhoto(event, num) {
    event.stopPropagation();
    const img = document.getElementById(`photo-${num}-img`);
    const placeholder = document.getElementById(`photo-${num}-placeholder`);
    img.src = '';
    img.classList.remove('loaded');
    placeholder.style.display = 'flex';
    document.getElementById(`photo-${num}-file`).value = '';
  }
  function addPhotoSlot() {
    photoCount++;
    const grid = document.getElementById('photo-grid');
    grid.appendChild(makePhotoSlot(photoCount));
  }
  function triggerBulkPhotoUpload() {
    const input = document.getElementById('bulk-photo-input');
    input.value = ''; // reset so same files can be re-selected
    input.click();
  }
  function bulkLoadPhotos(input) {
    const files = Array.from(input.files);
    if (!files.length) return;
    const grid = document.getElementById('photo-grid');
    // Step 1: Assign all slot numbers SYNCHRONOUSLY before any async work
    const assignments = []; // [{num, file}, ...]
    let searchFrom = 1;
    files.forEach(function(file) {
      let targetNum = null;
      // Find next empty slot starting from where we left off
      for (let i = searchFrom; i <= photoCount; i++) {
        const img = document.getElementById('photo-' + i + '-img');
        if (img && !img.classList.contains('loaded')) {
          targetNum = i;
          searchFrom = i + 1; // next search starts after this slot
          break;
        }
      }
      if (targetNum === null) {
        // No empty slot found — create a new one
        photoCount++;
        grid.appendChild(makePhotoSlot(photoCount));
        targetNum = photoCount;
        searchFrom = photoCount + 1;
      }
      assignments.push({ num: targetNum, file: file });
    });
    // Step 2: Now load each file into its pre-assigned slot
    assignments.forEach(function(a) {
      (function(num, f) {
        const reader = new FileReader();
        reader.onload = function(evt) {
          const img = document.getElementById('photo-' + num + '-img');
          const placeholder = document.getElementById('photo-' + num + '-placeholder');
          if (img) {
            img.src = evt.target.result;
            img.classList.add('loaded');
            img.setAttribute('data-local', '1');
          }
          if (placeholder) placeholder.style.display = 'none';
        };
        reader.readAsDataURL(f);
        uploadPhotoToStorage(num, f);
      })(a.num, a.file);
    });
  }
  // ── PROGRESS ──
  const sectionOrder = ['intro','insured','construction','occupancy','protection','exposure','loss','safety','recommendations','photos','summary','supp-manager','supp-restaurant','supp-woodworking','supp-warehouse','supp-autoservice','supp-sprinkler','supp-apartments','supp-addbuilding','gl-manager','gl-premises','gl-products','gl-fleet'];
  function updateProgress() {
    const current = document.querySelector('.nav-item.active');
    if (!current) return;
    const id = current.dataset.section;
    const idx = sectionOrder.indexOf(id);
    const pct = Math.round(((idx + 1) / sectionOrder.length) * 100);
    document.getElementById('progress-fill').style.width = pct + '%';
  }
  // ── SAVE / EXPORT ──
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  // PHASE 3 — AUTHENTICATION
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  let currentUser = null;
  let currentUserRole = 'inspector';
  let currentUserEmail = '';
  let authToken = null;
  async function doLogin() {
    const email = document.getElementById('login-email').value.trim();
    const password = document.getElementById('login-password').value;
    const btn = document.getElementById('login-btn');
    const errBox = document.getElementById('login-error');
    if (!email || !password) {
      showLoginError('Please enter your email and password.');
      return;
    }
    btn.disabled = true;
    btn.textContent = 'Signing in...';
    errBox.style.display = 'none';
    try {
      // Use Supabase JS client — handles CORS from file:// correctly
      const { data, error } = await _supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({ email, password });
      if (error) {
        let msg = error.message || 'Sign in failed.';
        // Surface common Edge-specific issues clearly
        if (msg.includes('fetch') || msg.includes('network') || msg.includes('Failed')) {
          msg = 'Network error — check your internet connection and that pop-ups are not blocked in Edge.';
        }
        if (msg.includes('crypto') || msg.includes('subtle')) {
          msg = 'Browser security error — please open this page over HTTPS (not as a local file) or try Chrome.';
        }
        showLoginError(msg);
        btn.disabled = false;
        btn.textContent = 'Sign In →';
        return;
      }
      authToken = data.session.access_token;
      currentUser = data.user;
      currentUserEmail = email;
      // Fetch profile for role
      const { data: profiles } = await _supabase
        .from('profiles')
        .select('role, full_name')
        .eq('id', currentUser.id);
      currentUserRole = profiles?.[0]?.role || 'inspector';
      const fullName = profiles?.[0]?.full_name || email.split('@')[0];
      // Auto-create profile if missing
      if (!profiles?.length) {
        await _supabase.from('profiles').insert({
          id: currentUser.id, email, role: 'inspector', full_name: fullName
        });
      }
      // Update HEADERS for raw fetch calls
      HEADERS['Authorization'] = 'Bearer ' + authToken;
      onLoginSuccess(fullName);
    } catch(e) {
      console.error('[SRC] Login error:', e);
      showLoginError('Connection error. Please try again.');
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.textContent = 'Sign In →';
    }
  }
  function onLoginSuccess(name) {
    // Login screen is /login.html — no overlay to hide
    // Show user badge
    const badge = document.getElementById('user-badge');
    const avatar = document.getElementById('user-avatar');
    const emailDisplay = document.getElementById('user-email-display');
    const rolePill = document.getElementById('user-role-pill');
    const logoutBtn = document.getElementById('btn-logout');
    badge.style.display = 'flex';
    logoutBtn.style.display = 'block';
    avatar.textContent = name.charAt(0).toUpperCase();
    emailDisplay.textContent = name;
    rolePill.textContent = currentUserRole;
    rolePill.className = 'user-role-pill ' + currentUserRole;
    // Update HEADERS with user auth token
    HEADERS['Authorization'] = 'Bearer ' + authToken;
    // Show inspector filter only for admins
    if (currentUserRole === 'admin') {
      const fi = document.getElementById('filter-inspector');
      if (fi) fi.style.display = 'block';
    }
    // Pre-fill inspector name field if empty
    const inspField = document.getElementById('inspector-name');
    if (inspField && !inspField.value) inspField.value = name;
    setDbStatus('connected', 'Connected');
    showToast('✓ Welcome, ' + name + ' (' + currentUserRole + ')');
    // Load reviewer list for QA dropdown
    loadReviewerList();
    // Only reset QA state to draft if no inspection is currently loaded
    if (!currentInspectionId) {
      applyQAState('draft');
    }
  }
  function showLoginError(msg) {
    const el = document.getElementById('login-error');
    el.textContent = msg;
    el.style.display = 'block';
  }
  async function doLogout() {
    if (!confirm('Sign out?')) return;
    try { await _supabase.auth.signOut(); } catch(e) {}
    window.location.replace('/login.html');
  }
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  // PHASE 4 — ENHANCED DASHBOARD
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  function updateDashStats(rows) {
    const total = rows.length;
    const high = rows.filter(r => (r.risk_quality||'').toLowerCase().includes('high') || (r.risk_quality||'').toLowerCase().includes('decline')).length;
    const mod  = rows.filter(r => (r.risk_quality||'').toLowerCase().includes('moderate') || (r.risk_quality||'').toLowerCase().includes('refer')).length;
    const low  = rows.filter(r => (r.risk_quality||'').toLowerCase().includes('low') || (r.risk_quality||'').toLowerCase().includes('acceptable') || (r.risk_quality||'').toLowerCase().includes('preferred')).length;
    document.getElementById('stat-total').textContent = total;
    document.getElementById('stat-high').textContent = high;
    document.getElementById('stat-mod').textContent = mod;
    document.getElementById('stat-low').textContent = low;
    document.getElementById('dash-stats-row').style.display = total > 0 ? 'grid' : 'none';
    document.getElementById('dash-filters').style.display = total > 0 ? 'flex' : 'none';
  }
  function populateFilterDropdowns(rows) {
    // Occupancy filter
    const occSel = document.getElementById('filter-occupancy');
    const occs = [...new Set(rows.map(r => r.occupancy_class).filter(Boolean))].sort();
    occSel.innerHTML = '<option value="">All Occupancies</option>' +
      occs.map(o => `<option value="${o}">${o}</option>`).join('');
    // Inspector filter (admin only)
    const inspSel = document.getElementById('filter-inspector');
    if (inspSel && currentUserRole === 'admin') {
      const insps = [...new Set(rows.map(r => r.inspector_name).filter(Boolean))].sort();
      inspSel.innerHTML = '<option value="">All Inspectors</option>' +
        insps.map(i => `<option value="${i}">${i}</option>`).join('');
    }
  }

  // PHASE 2 — SUPABASE DATABASE INTEGRATION
