  const SUPABASE_URL = 'https://lzsfmqbhrpsmnivxhggi.supabase.co';
  const SUPABASE_KEY = 'sb_publishable_C5KWTHt84OMXif4javqeOQ_rjFK0t83';
  const HEADERS = {
    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
    'apikey': SUPABASE_KEY,
    'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + SUPABASE_KEY,
    'Prefer': 'return=representation'
  };
  // Initialise Supabase JS client
  // Note: flowType 'implicit' used for broad browser compatibility (Chrome, Edge, Firefox, Safari)
  // persistSession uses localStorage — works on Netlify and local file in all major browsers
  const _supabase = supabase.createClient(SUPABASE_URL, SUPABASE_KEY, {
    auth: {
      autoRefreshToken: true,
      persistSession: true,
      detectSessionInUrl: false,
      flowType: 'implicit',
      storage: window.localStorage
    }
  });
  let allInspections = [];
  let currentInspectionId = null; // DB row UUID of loaded record
  // ── CONNECTION CHECK ──
  async function checkConnection() {
    setDbStatus('saving', 'Connecting...');
    try {
      const { error } = await _supabase.from('inspections').select('id').limit(1);
      if (!error) {
        setDbStatus('connected', 'Connected');
      } else if (error.code === '42P01') {
        setDbStatus('error', 'Run setup SQL');
      } else {
        setDbStatus('error', 'Error: ' + error.message);
      }
    } catch(e) {
      setDbStatus('error', 'Offline');
    }
  }
  function setDbStatus(state, label) {
    const dot = document.getElementById('db-dot');
    const lbl = document.getElementById('db-label');
    if (dot) { dot.className = 'db-dot ' + state; }
    if (lbl) lbl.textContent = label;
  }
  // ── COLLECT ALL FORM DATA ──
  function collectFormData() {
    const get = id => { const el = document.getElementById(id); return el ? el.value : ''; };
    var panels = document.querySelectorAll('.section-panel');
    // Walk every input/select/textarea and collect by id
    const fields = {};
    document.querySelectorAll('input[id], select[id], textarea[id]').forEach(el => {
      fields[el.id] = el.value;
    });
    // Collect selected radio/check pills
    const selected = {};
    document.querySelectorAll('.radio-group, .check-group').forEach((grp, i) => {
      const vals = [];
      grp.querySelectorAll('.selected').forEach(el => vals.push(el.textContent.trim()));
      const key = grp.closest('.field')?.querySelector('label')?.textContent?.trim()?.replace(/[^a-z0-9]/gi,'_').toLowerCase() || 'group_' + i;
      selected[key] = vals;
    });
    // Collect rating values
    const ratings = {};
    document.querySelectorAll('.rating-row').forEach(function(row) {
      var labelEl = row.querySelector('.rating-label');
      var label = labelEl ? labelEl.textContent.trim() : '';
      // Only look for sel button inside .rating-btns, not the whole row
      var btnsDiv = row.querySelector('.rating-btns');
      var sel = btnsDiv ? btnsDiv.querySelector('.rating-btn.sel') : null;
      if (label) ratings[label] = sel ? sel.textContent.trim() : null;
    });
    // Active supplements and GL modules
    const supplements = [...activeSupplements];
    const glModules = [...activeGL];
    // Key summary fields for dashboard display
    const summary = {
      inspection_id:  get('inspection-id') || 'INS-2026-0001',
      account_number: get('account-number') || '',
      policy_number:  get('policy-number') || '',
      inspection_date: get('inspection-date'),
      insured_name:   get('insured-name') || get('legal-entity') || '',
      location:       get('location-address') || get('street-address') || '',
      city:           get('city-location') || get('city') || '',
      province_state: get('province-location') || get('province') || '',
      occupancy_class: document.getElementById('occupancy-class-select')?.value || '',
      uw_recommendation: get('uw-recommendation') || '',
      risk_quality:   get('risk-quality-rating') || '',
      inspector_name: get('inspector-name') || '',
      lob:            get('line-of-business') || '',
    };
    // Collect pct-row tables (wall, roof, heating, AC, etc.)
    var pctRows = {};
    var pctContainerIds = ['wall-pct-rows', 'frame-pct-rows', 'rooftype-pct-rows', 'roof-pct-rows', 'deck-pct-rows', 'heat-pct-rows', 'ac-pct-rows', 'ext-finish-pct-rows', 'iso-pct-rows', 'bsmt-use-pct-rows'];
    pctContainerIds.forEach(function(cid) {
      var container = document.getElementById(cid);
      if (!container) return;
      var rows = [];
      container.querySelectorAll('.pct-row').forEach(function(row) {
        var sel = row.querySelector('select');
        var inp = row.querySelector('input[type="number"]');
        if (sel || inp) rows.push({ val: sel ? sel.value : '', pct: inp ? inp.value : '' });
      });
      pctRows[cid] = rows;
    });
    // Collect finish-row tables (floor, wall, ceiling)
    var finishRows = {};
    var finishContainerIds = ['floor-finish-rows', 'wall-finish-rows', 'ceiling-finish-rows'];
    finishContainerIds.forEach(function(cid) {
      var container = document.getElementById(cid);
      if (!container) return;
      var rows = [];
      container.querySelectorAll('.finish-row').forEach(function(row) {
        var sel  = row.querySelector('select');
        var note = row.querySelectorAll('input[type="text"]')[0];
        var pct  = row.querySelector('input[type="number"]');
        rows.push({ val: sel ? sel.value : '', note: note ? note.value : '', pct: pct ? pct.value : '' });
      });
      finishRows[cid] = rows;
    });
    // Collect safety rating notes
    var safetyNoteIds = [
      'safety-notes-written-safety-program-policy',
      'safety-notes-employee-safety-training-records',
      'safety-notes-general-housekeeping',
      'safety-notes-slip-trip-fall-prevention',
      'safety-notes-egress-emergency-exits',
      'safety-notes-emergency-action-plan-eap',
      'safety-notes-ppe-availability-and-use',
      'safety-notes-equipment-maintenance-program'
    ];
    var safetyNotes = {};
    safetyNoteIds.forEach(function(nid) {
      var el = document.getElementById(nid + '-text');
      if (el && el.value.trim()) safetyNotes[nid] = el.value.trim();
    });
    // Collect recommendation items from DOM
    var recData = [];
    var recListEl = document.getElementById('rec-list');
    if (recListEl) {
      recListEl.querySelectorAll('.rec-item').forEach(function(item, idx) {
        var priorityBtn = item.querySelector('.radio-btn.selected[data-level]');
        var levelMap = { high: 'High', med: 'Medium', low: 'Low' };
        var selects = item.querySelectorAll('select');
        var textareas = item.querySelectorAll('textarea');
        var notesEl = item.querySelector('.rec-notes-field') || textareas[1];
        var titleEl2 = item.querySelector('.rec-title-field');
        var refEl2 = item.querySelector('.rec-ref-field');
        recData.push({
          num: idx + 1,
          title: titleEl2 ? titleEl2.value.trim() : '',
          refnum: refEl2 ? refEl2.value.trim() : '',
          priority: priorityBtn ? (levelMap[priorityBtn.getAttribute('data-level')] || '') : '',
          type: selects[0] ? selects[0].value : '',
          desc: textareas[0] ? textareas[0].value.trim() : '',
          section: selects[1] ? selects[1].value : '',
          consequence: selects[3] ? selects[3].value : '',
          notes: notesEl ? notesEl.value.trim() : ''
        });
      });
    }
    return {
      ...summary,
      form_fields: fields,
      pill_selections: selected,
      rating_values: ratings,
      active_supplements: supplements,
      active_gl_modules: glModules,
      pct_rows: pctRows,
      finish_rows: finishRows,
      rec_items: recData,
      safety_notes: safetyNotes,
      saved_at: new Date().toISOString(),
      db_row_id: currentInspectionId
    };
  }
  // ── EXPORT PDF ──
  // Simple, reliable: shows all core sections + only active supplements.
  // Uses window.print() directly — no iframe complexity.
  function exportPDF() {
    // ── Use collectFormData() to read ALL field values reliably ──
    const data = collectFormData();
    const val = (v) => (v && v.trim && v.trim()) ? v.trim() : '—';
    document.getElementById('pdf-insp-id').textContent   = val(data.inspection_id);
    document.getElementById('pdf-insp-date').textContent = val(data.inspection_date);
    document.getElementById('pdf-insured').textContent   = val(data.insured_name) !== '—'
      ? val(data.insured_name)
      : val(data.form_fields['legal-entity']);
    document.getElementById('pdf-location').textContent  = (() => {
      const parts = [
        data.form_fields['street-address'] || data.form_fields['location-address'] || '',
        data.city || data.form_fields['city'] || '',
        data.province_state || data.form_fields['province'] || ''
      ].filter(v => v && v.trim());
      return parts.length ? parts.join(', ') : '—';
    })();
    document.getElementById('pdf-occupancy').textContent = val(data.occupancy_class) !== '—'
      ? val(data.occupancy_class)
      : val(data.form_fields['occupancy-class-select']);
    document.getElementById('pdf-inspector').textContent = val(data.inspector_name) !== '—'
      ? val(data.inspector_name)
      : val(data.form_fields['inspector-name']);
    // Add Photo 1 to cover page if it has been loaded
    const coverPhoto = document.getElementById('pdf-cover-photo');
    const photo1img  = document.getElementById('photo-1-img');
    if (coverPhoto && photo1img && photo1img.classList.contains('loaded') && photo1img.src) {
      coverPhoto.src = photo1img.src;
      coverPhoto.classList.remove('pdf-cover-photo-empty');
    } else if (coverPhoto) {
      coverPhoto.src = '';
      coverPhoto.classList.add('pdf-cover-photo-empty');
    }
    // Add sprinkler grade to cover if graded
    const spkGrade = document.getElementById('spk-final-grade')?.value;
    const spkScore = document.getElementById('spk-score')?.textContent;
    const spkWrap  = document.getElementById('pdf-sprinkler-grade-wrap');
    const spkEl    = document.getElementById('pdf-sprinkler-grade');
    if (spkWrap && spkEl && spkGrade && spkGrade !== '') {
      spkEl.textContent = 'Grade ' + spkGrade + (spkScore && spkScore !== '100' ? '  (Score: ' + spkScore + '/100)' : '');
      spkWrap.style.display = 'flex';
    } else if (spkWrap) {
      spkWrap.style.display = 'none';
    }
    const coverTitle = document.querySelector('.pdf-cover-title');
    if (coverTitle) coverTitle.textContent = 'Inspection Report';
    const panels = document.querySelectorAll('.section-panel');
    // Expand all design area cards
    document.querySelectorAll('.design-area-card').forEach(c => c.classList.add('expanded'));
    // Make all building card dividers visible (they use inline styles)
    document.querySelectorAll('#additional-buildings-container .divider').forEach(d => {
      d.style.display = 'block';
    });
    // Hide ALL supplement/GL sections first
    document.querySelectorAll('[id^="section-supp-"], [id^="section-gl-"]')
      .forEach(el => el.classList.add('supp-hide-print'));
    // Show ONLY the active ones
    activeSupplements.forEach(id => {
      const el = document.getElementById('section-supp-' + id);
      if (el) el.classList.remove('supp-hide-print');
    });
    activeGL.forEach(id => {
      const el = document.getElementById('section-gl-' + id);
      if (el) el.classList.remove('supp-hide-print');
    });
    window.print();
    // Restore everything after print dialog closes
    setTimeout(() => {
      document.querySelectorAll('.supp-hide-print')
        .forEach(el => el.classList.remove('supp-hide-print'));
      document.querySelectorAll('.design-area-card.expanded')
        .forEach(c => c.classList.remove('expanded'));
    }, 2500);
  }
    async function saveInspection() {
    setDbStatus('saving', 'Saving...');
    const data = collectFormData();
    // Build payload FIRST before any async calls
    const payload = {
      inspection_id:     data.inspection_id,
      account_number:    data.account_number || null,
      inspection_date:   data.inspection_date || null,
      insured_name:      data.insured_name,
      location:          data.location,
      city:              data.city,
      province_state:    data.province_state,
      occupancy_class:   data.occupancy_class,
      uw_recommendation: data.uw_recommendation,
      risk_quality:      data.risk_quality,
      inspector_name:    data.inspector_name,
      lob:               data.lob,
      user_id:           currentUser?.id || null,
      user_email:        currentUserEmail || null,
      form_data:         JSON.stringify({
        fields:      data.form_fields,
        pills:       data.pill_selections,
        ratings:     data.rating_values,
        supplements: data.active_supplements,
        gl_modules:  data.active_gl_modules,
        pct_rows:    data.pct_rows,
        finish_rows: data.finish_rows,
        rec_items:   data.rec_items,
        safety_notes: data.safety_notes,
      }),
      updated_at: new Date().toISOString()
    };
    try {
      let saveResult;
      if (currentInspectionId) {
        saveResult = await _supabase
          .from('inspections')
          .update(payload)
          .eq('id', currentInspectionId)
          .select();
      } else {
        saveResult = await _supabase
          .from('inspections')
          .insert(payload)
          .select();
      }
      const { data: result, error: saveError } = saveResult;
      if (!saveError) {
        if (!currentInspectionId && result?.[0]?.id) {
          currentInspectionId = result[0].id;
        }
        // Flush any pending photo uploads now that we have an inspection ID
        await flushPendingPhotoUploads();
        // Save photo metadata (captions, categories, storage paths)
        await savePhotoMetadata();
        setDbStatus('connected', 'Connected');
        showToast('✓ Saved to database — ' + data.inspection_id);
        // Only download local backup when explicitly requested, not on every save
      } else {
        console.error('Save error:', saveError);
        setDbStatus('error', 'Save failed');
        showToast('⚠ Database save failed — check console for details', 'warn');
      }
    } catch(e) {
      console.error('[SRC] Save error:', e);
      setDbStatus('error', 'Save error');
      showToast('⚠ Save error — check console for details', 'warn');
    }
  }
  async function saveAndDownload() {
    await saveInspection();
    const data = collectFormData();
    downloadLocalBackup(data.inspection_id);
  }
  // ── LOCAL HTML BACKUP (existing behaviour) ──
  function downloadLocalBackup(inspId) {
    const inputs = document.querySelectorAll('input, select, textarea');
    inputs.forEach(el => {
      if (el.type === 'checkbox' || el.type === 'radio') {
        el.setAttribute('checked', el.checked);
      } else {
        el.setAttribute('value', el.value);
        if (el.tagName === 'TEXTAREA') el.textContent = el.value;
        if (el.tagName === 'SELECT') {
          Array.from(el.options).forEach(opt => {
            opt.selected ? opt.setAttribute('selected','selected') : opt.removeAttribute('selected');
          });
        }
      }
    });
    const date = new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10);
    const filename = 'SRC-' + (inspId || 'INS') + '-' + date + '.html';
    const blob = new Blob([document.documentElement.outerHTML], { type: 'text/html;charset=utf-8' });
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = url; a.download = filename;
    document.body.appendChild(a); a.click();
    document.body.removeChild(a);
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
  }
  // ── DASHBOARD ──
  async function loadDashboard() {
    const wrap = document.getElementById('dashboard-table-wrap');
    wrap.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><div class="empty-icon">🔄</div>Loading...</div>';
    try {
      // Build query — include report_published so the Publish button renders correctly
      let query = _supabase
        .from('inspections')
        .select('id,inspection_id,account_number,policy_number,inspection_date,insured_name,city,province_state,occupancy_class,risk_quality,uw_recommendation,inspector_name,user_email,user_id,report_published,report_status,qa_reviewer,updated_at')
        .order('updated_at', { ascending: false })
        .limit(200);
      // Inspectors only see their own records; admins see everything
      if (currentUserRole !== 'admin' && currentUser) {
        query = query.eq('user_id', currentUser.id);
      }
      const { data: rows, error } = await query;
      if (error) throw error;
      allInspections = rows || [];
      updateDashStats(allInspections);
      populateFilterDropdowns(allInspections);
      renderDashboardTable(allInspections);
    } catch(e) {
      console.error('[SRC] Dashboard load error:', e);
      wrap.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><div class="empty-icon">⚠️</div>Could not load inspections.<br>' + (e.message || 'Check console for details.') + '</div>';
    }
  }
  function renderDashboardTable(rows) {
    const wrap = document.getElementById('dashboard-table-wrap');
    const count = document.getElementById('dashboard-count');
    if (count) count.textContent = rows.length + ' inspection' + (rows.length !== 1 ? 's' : '');
    if (!rows.length) {
      wrap.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><div class="empty-icon">📋</div>No inspections saved yet.<br>Complete a form and click Save to get started.</div>';
      return;
    }
    const riskClass = val => {
      if (!val) return 'na';
      const v = val.toLowerCase();
      if (v.includes('high') || v.includes('decline')) return 'high';
      if (v.includes('moderate') || v.includes('refer')) return 'moderate';
      if (v.includes('acceptable')) return 'acceptable';
      if (v.includes('low') || v.includes('preferred')) return 'low';
      return 'na';
    };
    const rows_html = rows.map(r => {
      const date = r.inspection_date ? new Date(r.inspection_date).toLocaleDateString('en-CA') : '—';
      const updated = r.updated_at ? new Date(r.updated_at).toLocaleDateString('en-CA') : '—';
      const loc = [r.city, r.province_state].filter(Boolean).join(', ') || '—';
      const rq = r.risk_quality || '—';
      return `<tr>
        <td>${r.account_number ? `<span style="font-family:'IBM Plex Mono',monospace;font-size:11px;background:var(--gold-pale);color:var(--navy);padding:2px 8px;border-radius:10px;">${r.account_number}</span>` : '—'}</td>
        <td>${r.policy_number ? `<span style="font-family:'IBM Plex Mono',monospace;font-size:11px;background:#ebf4ff;color:#2b6cb0;padding:2px 8px;border-radius:10px;">${r.policy_number}</span>` : '—'}</td>
        <td><strong>${r.inspection_id || '—'}</strong></td>
        <td>${date}</td>
        <td>${r.insured_name || '—'}</td>
        <td>${loc}</td>
        <td>${r.occupancy_class || '—'}</td>
        <td>${r.inspector_name || '—'}</td>
        <td><span class="risk-badge ${riskClass(rq)}">${rq}</span></td>
        <td>${updated}</td>
        <td style="white-space:nowrap;">
          <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:3px;align-items:flex-start;">
            <div style="display:flex;gap:3px;">
              <button class="btn-load-insp" style="padding:4px 8px;font-size:10px;min-height:36px;min-width:50px;" onclick="event.stopPropagation();event.preventDefault();loadInspection('${r.id}')">Load</button>
              <span style="font-size:10px;font-weight:700;padding:2px 8px;border-radius:10px;margin-left:4px;${
                r.report_status === 'approved'  ? 'background:#F0FFF4;color:#276749;' :
                r.report_status === 'inreview'  ? 'background:#FAF5FF;color:#6B46C1;' :
                r.report_status === 'submitted' ? 'background:#FFF3E0;color:#C05621;' :
                r.report_status === 'returned'  ? 'background:#FEE2E2;color:#C53030;' :
                'background:rgba(255,255,255,0.1);color:#7a9ab5;'
              }">${r.report_status ? r.report_status.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + r.report_status.slice(1) : 'Draft'}${r.qa_reviewer ? ' — ' + r.qa_reviewer : ''}</span>
              ${(r.report_status === 'submitted') ? '<select id="assign-qa-' + r.id + '" style="font-size:10px;padding:3px 6px;border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:5px;margin-left:4px;" onchange="assignToReviewer(\'' + r.id + '\', this.value)"><option value="">— Assign to Reviewer —</option>' + qaReviewerList.map(function(rev){return '<option value="' + (rev.full_name||rev.email) + '">' + (rev.full_name||rev.email) + '</option>';}).join('') + '</select>' : ''}
              <button class="btn-load-insp" style="padding:4px 8px;font-size:10px;${r.report_published ? 'background:#276749;color:white;' : 'background:#f0fff4;color:#276749;border:1px solid #276749;'}"
                onclick="togglePublishReport('${r.id}', ${r.report_published ? 'true' : 'false'}, '${r.inspection_id || ''}', '${r.insured_name ? r.insured_name.replace(/'/g, '') : ''}')">
                ${r.report_published ? 'Unpublish' : 'Publish'}
              </button>
              <button class="btn-del-insp" style="padding:4px 8px;font-size:10px;margin-left:0;" onclick="deleteInspection('${r.id}','${r.inspection_id}')">✕</button>
            </div>
            ${r.report_published ? `<a href="/report?ref=${r.inspection_id}" target="_blank"
              style="font-size:10px;color:#2b6cb0;text-decoration:none;">&#x1F517; View Report</a>` : ''}
          </div>
        </td>
      </tr>`;
    }).join('');
    wrap.innerHTML = `<div style="overflow-x:auto;"><table class="insp-table" style="min-width:1100px;width:100%;">
      <thead><tr>
        <th>Account #</th><th>Policy #</th><th>Insp. ID</th><th>Date</th><th>Insured</th><th>Location</th>
        <th>Occupancy</th><th>Inspector</th><th>Risk</th><th>Last Saved</th><th>Actions</th>
      </tr></thead>
      <tbody>${rows_html}</tbody>
    </table></div>`;
  }
  function filterDashboard() {
    const q     = document.getElementById('dashboard-search').value.toLowerCase();
    const risk  = document.getElementById('filter-risk')?.value || '';
    const occ   = document.getElementById('filter-occupancy')?.value || '';
    const insp  = document.getElementById('filter-inspector')?.value || '';
    const year  = document.getElementById('filter-year')?.value || '';
    const riskClass = val => {
      if (!val) return 'na';
      const v = val.toLowerCase();
      if (v.includes('high') || v.includes('decline')) return 'high';
      if (v.includes('moderate') || v.includes('refer')) return 'moderate';
      if (v.includes('acceptable')) return 'acceptable';
      if (v.includes('low') || v.includes('preferred')) return 'low';
      return 'na';
    };
    let filtered = allInspections.filter(r => {
      const matchQ    = !q || (r.inspection_id||'').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
                        (r.account_number||'').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
                        (r.policy_number||'').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
                        (r.insured_name||'').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
                        (r.city||'').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
                        (r.occupancy_class||'').toLowerCase().includes(q);
      const matchRisk = !risk || riskClass(r.risk_quality) === risk;
      const matchOcc  = !occ  || (r.occupancy_class||'') === occ;
      const matchInsp = !insp || (r.inspector_name||'') === insp;
      const matchYear = !year || (r.inspection_date||'').startsWith(year);
      return matchQ && matchRisk && matchOcc && matchInsp && matchYear;
    });
    renderDashboardTable(filtered);
  }
  // ── LOAD INSPECTION FROM DB ──
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  // INSPECTION REQUESTS
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  // ── INSPECTION REQUESTS ──
  // Cached inspector list for assign dropdown
  let _inspectorList = [];
  async function loadInspectorList() {
    try {
      const { data } = await _supabase.from('profiles').select('full_name, email').order('full_name');
      _inspectorList = (data || []).filter(p => p.full_name || p.email);
    } catch(e) { _inspectorList = []; }
  }
  async function loadRequests() {
    const wrap = document.getElementById('requests-wrap');
    const tbl  = document.getElementById('requests-table-wrap');
    wrap.style.display = 'block';
    tbl.innerHTML = '<div style="padding:20px;text-align:center;color:var(--slate);">⏳ Loading requests...</div>';
    wrap.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
    // Load inspectors for dropdown
    await loadInspectorList();
    try {
      // Build query — admins see all requests, inspectors only see requests assigned to them
      let reqQuery = _supabase
        .from('inspection_requests')
        .select('*')
        .order('submitted_at', { ascending: false });
      if (currentUserRole !== 'admin') {
        // Inspectors see requests assigned to them by name, plus all unassigned pending ones
        const inspectorName = document.getElementById('inspector-name')?.value?.trim() || currentUserEmail;
        reqQuery = reqQuery.or(`assigned_to.eq.${inspectorName},and(status.eq.Pending,assigned_to.is.null)`);
      }
      const { data: rows, error } = await reqQuery;
      if (error) throw error;
      if (!rows || !rows.length) {
        tbl.innerHTML = '<div style="padding:20px;text-align:center;color:var(--slate);">No inspection requests yet.</div>';
        return;
      }
      const urgencyColor = u => {
        if (!u) return '#888';
        if (u.includes('Urgent'))   return '#e53e3e';
        if (u.includes('Priority')) return '#dd6b20';
        return '#2f855a';
      };
      const statusBadge = s => {
        const colors = {
          'Pending':    'background:#fff3e0;color:#dd6b20;border:1px solid #dd6b20;',
          'Assigned':   'background:#ebf4ff;color:#2b6cb0;border:1px solid #2b6cb0;',
          'Converted':  'background:#f0fff4;color:#276749;border:1px solid #2f855a;',
          'Completed':  'background:#f0fff4;color:#276749;border:1px solid #2f855a;',
          'Reassigned': 'background:#faf5ff;color:#6b46c1;border:1px solid #805ad5;',
        };
        const style = colors[s] || 'background:#f7f7f7;color:#888;border:1px solid #ccc;';
        return `<span style="font-size:10px;font-weight:700;padding:2px 8px;border-radius:10px;${style}">${s || '—'}</span>`;
      };
      // Inspector options for dropdown
      const inspOpts = _inspectorList.length
        ? _inspectorList.map(p => `<option value="${p.full_name || p.email}">${p.full_name || p.email}</option>`).join('')
        : '<option value="">— No inspectors found —</option>';
      const rows_html = rows.map(r => {
        const date = r.submitted_at ? new Date(r.submitted_at).toLocaleDateString('en-CA') : '—';
        const pref = r.preferred_date ? new Date(r.preferred_date + 'T00:00:00').toLocaleDateString('en-CA') : '—';
        const assignedTo = r.assigned_to
          ? `<span style="font-size:11px;font-weight:600;color:var(--navy);">&#x1F464; ${r.assigned_to}</span>`
          : `<span style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-light);font-style:italic;">Unassigned</span>`;
        const rJson = JSON.stringify(r).split('"').join('&quot;');
        const isCompleted = r.status === 'Completed';
        return `<tr style="${isCompleted ? 'opacity:0.6;' : ''}">
          <td><span style="font-family:'IBM Plex Mono',monospace;font-size:11px;background:var(--gold-pale);color:var(--navy);padding:2px 8px;border-radius:10px;">${r.request_ref || '—'}</span></td>
          <td style="font-size:12px;">${date}</td>
          <td style="word-break:break-word;"><strong style="font-size:12px;">${r.insured_name || '—'}</strong><br>
              <span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--slate)">${[r.city, r.province].filter(Boolean).join(', ')}</span></td>
          <td style="font-size:12px;">${r.occupancy_type || '—'}</td>
          <td style="font-size:12px;">${r.purpose || '—'}</td>
          <td><span style="font-size:11px;font-weight:600;color:${urgencyColor(r.urgency)}">${r.urgency ? r.urgency.split('—')[0].trim() : '—'}</span></td>
          <td>${statusBadge(r.status)}</td>
          <td>
            ${assignedTo}
            <div style="margin-top:6px;display:flex;gap:4px;align-items:center;">
              <select id="assign-sel-${r.id}" style="font-size:10px;padding:2px 4px;border-radius:6px;border:1px solid var(--border);max-width:110px;">
                <option value="">— Assign to —</option>
                ${inspOpts}
              </select>
              <button class="btn-load-insp" style="font-size:10px;padding:3px 8px;white-space:nowrap;"
                onclick="assignInspector('${r.id}', '${r.status}')">
                ${r.assigned_to ? '&#x21BB; Reassign' : 'Assign'}
              </button>
            </div>
          </td>
          <td style="font-size:12px;">${pref}</td>
          <td style="white-space:nowrap;">
            <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:4px;">
              <button class="btn-load-insp" onclick="convertRequest(${rJson})"
                style="font-size:11px;">&#x21AA; Convert</button>
              <button class="btn-del-insp" onclick="markCompleted('${r.id}')"
                style="font-size:11px;${isCompleted ? 'background:#ccc;color:#888;cursor:not-allowed;' : ''}">
                ${isCompleted ? '&#x2713; Done' : '&#x2713; Complete'}</button>
              ${r.status === 'Completed' || r.status === 'Converted'
                ? `<button class="btn-load-insp" style="font-size:10px;padding:3px 8px;background:#fff3e0;color:#dd6b20;border-color:#dd6b20;"
                    onclick="reopenRequest('${r.id}')">&#x21BA; Reopen</button>`
                : ''}
            </div>
          </td>
        </tr>`;
      }).join('');
      tbl.innerHTML = `
        <div style="overflow-x:auto;width:100%;">
        <table class="insp-table" style="width:100%;table-layout:fixed;min-width:1100px;">
          <colgroup>
            <col style="width:110px">  <!-- Ref # -->
            <col style="width:90px">   <!-- Submitted -->
            <col style="width:200px">  <!-- Property -->
            <col style="width:130px">  <!-- Occupancy -->
            <col style="width:110px">  <!-- Purpose -->
            <col style="width:80px">   <!-- Urgency -->
            <col style="width:90px">   <!-- Status -->
            <col style="width:180px">  <!-- Assigned To -->
            <col style="width:100px">  <!-- Preferred Date -->
            <col style="width:130px">  <!-- Actions -->
          </colgroup>
          <thead><tr>
            <th>Ref #</th><th>Submitted</th><th>Property</th>
            <th>Occupancy</th><th>Purpose</th><th>Urgency</th><th>Status</th>
            <th>Assigned To</th><th>Preferred Date</th><th>Actions</th>
          </tr></thead>
          <tbody>${rows_html}</tbody>
        </table>
        </div>
        <div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-light);margin-top:8px;padding:0 4px;">
          &#x21BB; Reassign resets status to Assigned. &#x21BA; Reopen resets Completed requests back to Pending.
        </div>`;
    } catch(e) {
      console.error(e);
      tbl.innerHTML = '<div style="padding:20px;color:#e53e3e;">Failed to load requests: ' + (e.message || e) + '</div>';
    }
  }
  async function assignInspector(id, currentStatus) {
    const sel = document.getElementById('assign-sel-' + id);
    const inspector = sel ? sel.value.trim() : '';
    if (!inspector) { showToast('Please select an inspector first', 'warn'); return; }
    // If already assigned to someone, this is a reassignment
    const isReassign = currentStatus === 'Assigned' || currentStatus === 'Converted';
    const newStatus = isReassign ? 'Reassigned' : 'Assigned';
    try {
      const { error } = await _supabase
        .from('inspection_requests')
        .update({ assigned_to: inspector, status: newStatus })
        .eq('id', id);
      if (error) throw error;
      showToast(isReassign
        ? '✓ Request reassigned to ' + inspector
        : '✓ Assigned to ' + inspector);
      loadRequests();
    } catch(e) {
      showToast('⚠ Failed to assign: ' + (e.message || e), 'warn');
    }
  }
  async function markCompleted(id) {
    try {
      const { error } = await _supabase
        .from('inspection_requests')
        .update({ status: 'Completed' })
        .eq('id', id);
      if (error) throw error;
      showToast('✓ Request marked as Completed');
      loadRequests();
    } catch(e) {
      showToast('⚠ Failed to update: ' + (e.message || e), 'warn');
    }
  }
  async function reopenRequest(id) {
    if (!confirm('Reopen this request and reset status to Pending?')) return;
    try {
      const { error } = await _supabase
        .from('inspection_requests')
        .update({ status: 'Pending', assigned_to: null })
        .eq('id', id);
      if (error) throw error;
      showToast('✓ Request reopened — status reset to Pending');
      loadRequests();
    } catch(e) {
      showToast('⚠ Failed to reopen: ' + (e.message || e), 'warn');
    }
  }
  async function updateRequestStatus(id, status) {
    try {
      await _supabase.from('inspection_requests').update({ status }).eq('id', id);
      showToast('✓ Request updated to ' + status);
      loadRequests();
    } catch(e) {
      showToast('⚠ Failed to update status', 'warn');
    }
  }
  function convertRequest(r) {
    // Pre-populate the inspection form with data from the request
    closeDashboard();
    showSection('intro', document.querySelector('[data-section="intro"]'));
    // Give the form a moment to become visible then populate
    setTimeout(() => {
      const set = (id, val) => { const el = document.getElementById(id); if (el && val) el.value = val; };
      // Generate a new inspection ID
      const now = new Date();
      const newId = 'INS-' + now.getFullYear() + '-' + String(now.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0') + String(now.getDate()).padStart(2,'0') + '-' + String(Math.floor(Math.random()*900)+100);
      set('inspection-id', newId);
      const badge = document.getElementById('inspection-id-badge');
      if (badge) badge.textContent = newId;
      set('account-number',  r.account_number);
      set('policy-number',   r.policy_number);
      set('inspection-date', new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]);
      // Insured section
      set('legal-entity',    r.insured_name);
      set('street-address',  r.address);
      set('city',            r.city);
      set('province',        r.province);
      set('postal-code',     r.postal_code);
      // Purpose of inspection
      const purposeSel = document.querySelector('#section-intro select');
      if (purposeSel && r.purpose) {
        Array.from(purposeSel.options).forEach(o => { if (o.text === r.purpose) purposeSel.value = o.value; });
      }
      // ── Auto-activate supplements from request ──
      var svcText = (r.special_instructions || '') + ' ' + (r.comments || '');
      var svcKeyMap = {
        'Sprinkler':    'sprinkler',
        'Apartments':   'apartments',
        'Restaurant':   'restaurant',
        'Warehouse':    'warehouse',
        'Woodworking':  'woodworking',
        'Auto Service': 'autoservice',
      };
      Object.keys(svcKeyMap).forEach(function(keyword) {
        if (svcText.indexOf(keyword) !== -1) {
          var suppId = svcKeyMap[keyword];
          // Use the proper toggleSupplement function if not already active
          if (!activeSupplements.has(suppId)) {
            toggleSupplement(suppId);
          }
        }
      });
      // Show source request banner
      var srcBanner = document.getElementById('source-request-banner');
      var srcRef = document.getElementById('source-request-ref');
      var srcSvcs = document.getElementById('source-request-services');
      var srcDetail = document.getElementById('source-request-detail');
      if (srcBanner && srcRef) {
        srcRef.textContent = r.request_ref || '—';
        // Extract services from special_instructions
        var siText = r.special_instructions || '';
        var svcLine = siText.indexOf('SERVICES REQUESTED:') !== -1
          ? siText.substring(siText.indexOf('SERVICES REQUESTED:'))
          : '';
        if (srcSvcs) srcSvcs.textContent = svcLine ? '| ' + svcLine.split('\n')[0] : '';
        if (srcDetail) {
          srcDetail.textContent =
            'Requestor: ' + (r.requestor_name || '—') + ' (' + (r.requestor_company || '—') + ')\n' +
            'Submitted: ' + (r.submitted_at ? r.submitted_at.substring(0,10) : '—') + '\n' +
            'Urgency: ' + (r.urgency || '—') + '\n' +
            'Site Contact: ' + (r.site_contact || '—') + '\n' +
            'Instructions: ' + (r.special_instructions || '—') + '\n' +
            'Comments: ' + (r.comments || '—');
        }
        srcBanner.style.display = 'block';
      }
      showToast('✓ Form pre-populated from request ' + r.request_ref);
      // Mark request as Converted in database
      _supabase.from('inspection_requests')
        .update({ status: 'Converted' })
        .eq('id', r.id)
        .then(({ error }) => { if (error) console.warn('Could not update request status:', error.message); });
    }, 300);
  }
    async function loadInspection(dbId) {
    if (window._loadInProgress) {
      return;
    }
    window._loadInProgress = true;
    showToast('⏳ Loading inspection...');
    try {
      const { data: rows, error: loadErr } = await _supabase
        .from('inspections').select('*').eq('id', dbId).limit(1);
      if (loadErr) throw loadErr;
      if (!rows?.length) { showToast('⚠ Record not found', 'warn'); return; }
      const rec = rows[0];
      currentInspectionId = rec.id;
      // Parse form_data — handle both old (form_fields) and new (fields) key formats
      let fd = {};
      try { fd = JSON.parse(rec.form_data || '{}'); } catch(e) { fd = {}; }
      const fields = fd.fields || fd.form_fields || {};
      // ── Restore all input/select/textarea fields ──
      Object.entries(fields).forEach(([id, val]) => {
        const el = document.getElementById(id);
        if (!el || el.tagName === 'BUTTON') return;
        try {
          el.value = val;
          if (el.id === 'inspection-id') {
            const badge = document.getElementById('inspection-id-badge');
            if (badge) badge.textContent = val;
          }
        } catch(e) { /* skip unrestorable fields */ }
      });
      // ── Restore pill selections (radio-btn / check-btn) ──
      const pills = fd.pills || fd.pill_selections || {};
      Object.entries(pills).forEach(([key, vals]) => {
        if (!Array.isArray(vals)) return;
        // Find the group matching this key
        document.querySelectorAll('.radio-group, .check-group').forEach(grp => {
          const label = grp.closest('.field')?.querySelector('label')?.textContent?.trim()
                          ?.replace(/[^a-z0-9]/gi,'_').toLowerCase();
          if (label !== key) return;
          grp.querySelectorAll('.radio-btn, .check-btn').forEach(btn => {
            const txt = btn.textContent.trim();
            if (vals.includes(txt)) {
              btn.classList.add('selected');
            } else {
              btn.classList.remove('selected');
            }
          });
        });
      });
      // ── Restore hazard detail panels ──
      const hazMap = {
        'Cooking / Open Flame': 'cooking',
        'Welding / Cutting':    'welding',
        'Spray Painting / Coating': 'spray',
        'Chemical Mixing':      'chemical',
        'Woodworking / Dust':   'wooddust',
        'Compressed Gas':       'compgas',
        'Flammable Liquid Storage': 'flamliq',
        'Cryogenics':           'cryogen',
        'Printing / Ink':       'printing'
      };
      const hazGroup = document.getElementById('haz-processes');
      if (hazGroup) {
        hazGroup.querySelectorAll('.check-btn').forEach(btn => {
          const key = hazMap[btn.textContent.trim()];
          if (!key) return;
          const panel = document.getElementById('haz-detail-' + key);
          if (panel) panel.style.display = btn.classList.contains('selected') ? 'block' : 'none';
        });
      }
      // ── Restore rating buttons ──
      const ratings = fd.ratings || fd.rating_values || {};
      document.querySelectorAll('.rating-row').forEach(function(row) {
        var labelEl = row.querySelector('.rating-label');
        var label = labelEl ? labelEl.textContent.trim() : '';
        // Always clear ALL buttons in the row first (including stale Notes btn state)
        row.querySelectorAll('button').forEach(function(b) { b.classList.remove('sel'); });
        if (!label || !ratings[label]) return;
        var ratingVal2 = String(ratings[label]);
        // Only restore valid numeric ratings 1-5
        var validRatings = {'1':true,'2':true,'3':true,'4':true,'5':true};
        if (!validRatings[ratingVal2]) return;
        // Only add sel to actual .rating-btn buttons
        row.querySelectorAll('.rating-btn').forEach(function(btn) {
          if (btn.textContent.trim() === ratingVal2) btn.classList.add('sel');
        });
      });
      // ── Restore active supplements ──
      // First deactivate any currently active supplements
      [...activeSupplements].forEach(id => { if (activeSupplements.has(id)) toggleSupplement(id); });
      (fd.supplements || fd.active_supplements || []).forEach(id => {
        if (!activeSupplements.has(id)) toggleSupplement(id);
      });
      // ── Restore active GL modules ──
      [...activeGL].forEach(id => { if (activeGL.has(id)) toggleGL(id); });
      (fd.gl_modules || fd.active_gl_modules || []).forEach(id => {
        if (!activeGL.has(id)) toggleGL(id);
      });
      // ── Restore pct-row tables ──
      var pctRows = fd.pct_rows || {};
      Object.entries(pctRows).forEach(function([cid, rows]) {
        var container = document.getElementById(cid);
        if (!container || !rows.length) return;
        // Clear existing rows except the first, then repopulate
        var existing = container.querySelectorAll('.pct-row');
        // Add extra rows if needed
        while (container.querySelectorAll('.pct-row').length < rows.length) {
          // Determine type from container id
          var typeMap = {
            'wall-pct-rows':'wall','frame-pct-rows':'frame','rooftype-pct-rows':'rooftype',
            'roof-pct-rows':'roof','deck-pct-rows':'deck','heat-pct-rows':'heat',
            'ac-pct-rows':'ac','ext-finish-pct-rows':'extfinish',
            'iso-pct-rows':'isoclass','bsmt-use-pct-rows':'bsmtuse'
          };
          addPctRowTo(cid, typeMap[cid] || 'wall');
        }
        // Populate values
        var pctRowEls = container.querySelectorAll('.pct-row');
        rows.forEach(function(r, i) {
          if (!pctRowEls[i]) return;
          var sel = pctRowEls[i].querySelector('select');
          var inp = pctRowEls[i].querySelector('input[type="number"]');
          if (sel && r.val) sel.value = r.val;
          if (inp && r.pct) inp.value = r.pct;
        });
      });
      // ── Restore finish-row tables ──
      var finishRows = fd.finish_rows || {};
      var finishTypeMap = {'floor-finish-rows':'floor','wall-finish-rows':'wall','ceiling-finish-rows':'ceiling'};
      Object.entries(finishRows).forEach(function([cid, rows]) {
        var container = document.getElementById(cid);
        if (!container || !rows.length) return;
        while (container.querySelectorAll('.finish-row').length < rows.length) {
          addFinishRowTo(cid, finishTypeMap[cid] || 'floor');
        }
        var finRowEls = container.querySelectorAll('.finish-row');
        rows.forEach(function(r, i) {
          if (!finRowEls[i]) return;
          var sel  = finRowEls[i].querySelector('select');
          var note = finRowEls[i].querySelectorAll('input[type="text"]')[0];
          var pct  = finRowEls[i].querySelector('input[type="number"]');
          if (sel  && r.val)  sel.value  = r.val;
          if (note && r.note) note.value = r.note;
          if (pct  && r.pct)  pct.value  = r.pct;
        });
      });
      // ── Restore safety rating notes ──
      var savedSafetyNotes = fd.safety_notes || {};
      Object.keys(savedSafetyNotes).forEach(function(nid) {
        var el = document.getElementById(nid + '-text');
        if (el && savedSafetyNotes[nid]) {
          el.value = savedSafetyNotes[nid];
        }
      });
      // ── Restore recommendation items ──
      var savedRecs = fd.rec_items || [];
      if (savedRecs.length) {
        // Clear existing recs and rebuild from saved data
        var recListEl2 = document.getElementById('rec-list');
        if (recListEl2) {
          // Remove all except first
          var existingRecs = recListEl2.querySelectorAll('.rec-item');
          existingRecs.forEach(function(el, i) { if (i > 0) el.remove(); });
          savedRecs.forEach(function(r, idx2) {
            if (idx2 > 0) { addRecommendation(); }
            var item = recListEl2.querySelectorAll('.rec-item')[idx2];
            if (!item) return;
            // Set priority
            if (r.priority) {
              var levelMap2 = { 'High': 'high', 'Medium': 'med', 'Low': 'low' };
              var level = levelMap2[r.priority] || 'high';
              var priorityLbl = item.querySelector('[data-level="' + level + '"]');
              if (priorityLbl) {
                setRecPriority(priorityLbl, 'rec-' + (idx2+1), level);
              }
            }
            // Set type (first select)
            var sels2 = item.querySelectorAll('select');
            if (sels2[0] && r.type) sels2[0].value = r.type;
            if (sels2[1] && r.section) sels2[1].value = r.section;
            if (sels2[3] && r.consequence) sels2[3].value = r.consequence;
            // Set description (first textarea)
            var tas2 = item.querySelectorAll('textarea');
            if (tas2[0] && r.desc) tas2[0].value = r.desc;
            // Set notes
            var notesEl2 = item.querySelector('.rec-notes-field') || tas2[1];
            if (notesEl2 && r.notes) notesEl2.value = r.notes;
            var titleEl3 = item.querySelector('.rec-title-field');
            if (titleEl3 && r.title) titleEl3.value = r.title;
            var refEl3 = item.querySelector('.rec-ref-field');
            if (refEl3 && r.refnum) refEl3.value = r.refnum;
          });
        }
      }
      // ── Restore conditional sections ──
      if (document.getElementById('basement-area') &&
          document.getElementById('basement-area').value) toggleBasementUse();
      if (document.getElementById('mezzanine-present') &&
          document.getElementById('mezzanine-present').value === 'Yes') toggleMezzanine();
      if (document.getElementById('elev-passenger-count') ||
          document.getElementById('elev-freight-count')) toggleElevDetails();
      // ── Restore top-level fields from record columns (fallback) ──
      const setField = (id, val) => {
        const el = document.getElementById(id);
        if (el && val) el.value = val;
      };
      setField('inspection-id',   rec.inspection_id);
      setField('inspection-date', rec.inspection_date);
      setField('inspector-name',  rec.inspector_name);
      setField('legal-entity',    rec.insured_name);
      setField('city',            rec.city);
      setField('province',        rec.province_state);
      // ── Update header badges explicitly (oninput doesn't fire on programmatic set) ──
      const inspIdBadge = document.getElementById('inspection-id-badge');
      if (inspIdBadge && rec.inspection_id) inspIdBadge.textContent = rec.inspection_id;
      const acctBadge = document.getElementById('account-badge');
      const acctField = document.getElementById('account-number');
      // account_number comes from the record column OR from form_fields
      var acctVal = rec.account_number || (fields && fields['account-number']) || '';
      if (acctField) acctField.value = acctVal;
      if (acctBadge) {
        if (acctVal) {
          acctBadge.textContent = acctVal;
          acctBadge.style.display = 'block';
        } else {
          acctBadge.textContent = '';
          acctBadge.style.display = 'none';
        }
      }
      // Load photos from Supabase Storage
      if (rec.photo_data) {
        loadPhotosFromStorage(rec.photo_data);
      }
      // Restore QA state
      currentReportStatus = rec.report_status || 'draft';
      currentQAReviewer   = rec.qa_reviewer   || '';
      currentQANotes      = rec.qa_notes      || '';
      currentQADate       = rec.qa_date       || '';
      // Restore QA notes display fields
      var qaNotesEl = document.getElementById('qa-notes');
      if (qaNotesEl && currentQANotes) qaNotesEl.value = currentQANotes;
      var returnNotesEl = document.getElementById('qa-return-notes-display');
      if (returnNotesEl && currentQANotes) returnNotesEl.textContent = currentQANotes;
      var approvedByEl = document.getElementById('qa-approved-by-label');
      if (approvedByEl) approvedByEl.textContent = 'Approved by ' + (currentQAReviewer || '—') + ' on ' + (currentQADate || '—');
      applyQAState(currentReportStatus);
      closeDashboard();
      // Always show print/report buttons when a file is loaded
      var btnGrp = document.getElementById('report-btn-group');
      if (btnGrp) btnGrp.style.display = 'flex';
      setTimeout(function() {
        showSection('intro', document.querySelector('[data-section="intro"]'));
        // Force repaint on Chrome Android
        document.body.style.opacity = '0.99';
        setTimeout(function() {
          document.body.style.opacity = '1';
          applyQAState(currentReportStatus);
        }, 50);
      }, 50);
      showToast('✓ Loaded — ' + rec.inspection_id);
    } catch(e) {
      console.error('Load inspection error:', e);
      showToast('⚠ Failed to load: ' + (e.message || 'Check console for details'), 'warn');
    } finally {
      // Release lock after 1 second to prevent accidental double-tap loads
      setTimeout(function() { window._loadInProgress = false; }, 1500);
    }
  }
  // ── DELETE INSPECTION ──
  async function deleteInspection(dbId, inspId) {
    if (!confirm('Delete inspection ' + inspId + '? This cannot be undone.')) return;
    try {
      const { error } = await _supabase.from('inspections').delete().eq('id', dbId);
      if (!error) {
        showToast('✓ Deleted — ' + inspId);
        loadDashboard();
      } else {
        showToast('⚠ Delete failed: ' + error.message, 'warn');
      }
    } catch(e) {
      showToast('⚠ Delete failed — offline?', 'warn');
    }
  }
  // ── NEW INSPECTION ──
  function newInspection() {
    if (!confirm('Start a new inspection? Any unsaved changes will be lost.')) return;
    currentInspectionId = null;
    closeDashboard();
    location.reload();
  }
  function openDashboard() {
    document.getElementById('dashboard-modal').style.display = 'flex';
    loadDashboard();
  }
  function closeDashboard() {
    var modal = document.getElementById('dashboard-modal');
    if (!modal) return;
    modal.style.display = 'none';
  }
  // ── TOAST (updated to support warn style) ──
  function showToast(msg, type) {
    let toast = document.getElementById('save-toast');
    if (!toast) {
      toast = document.createElement('div');
      toast.id = 'save-toast';
      toast.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;bottom:80px;left:50%;transform:translateX(-50%);padding:10px 24px;border-radius:8px;font-size:13px;font-family:IBM Plex Sans,sans-serif;z-index:9999;box-shadow:0 4px 20px rgba(0,0,0,0.25);transition:opacity 0.4s;white-space:nowrap;';
      document.body.appendChild(toast);
    }
    toast.style.background = type === 'warn' ? '#c47a1a' : '#1e7e5a';
    toast.style.color = '#ffffff';
    toast.textContent = msg;
    toast.style.opacity = '1';
    setTimeout(() => { toast.style.opacity = '0'; }, 3500);
  }
    // ── COUNTRY / OSHA VISIBILITY ──
  function syncCountry(val) {
    // Keep both dropdowns in sync
    document.getElementById('country-mailing').value = val;
    document.getElementById('country-location').value = val;
    const oshaCard = document.getElementById('osha-card');
    if (val === 'US') {
      oshaCard.style.display = 'block';
      oshaCard.style.animation = 'fadeIn 0.25s ease';
    } else {
      oshaCard.style.display = 'none';
    }
  }

  function toggleDesignArea(id) {
    const card = document.getElementById('design-area-' + id);
    card.classList.toggle('expanded');
  }
  function updateDesignAreaMeta(id) {
    const hazard = document.getElementById('da-hazard-' + id)?.value || '';
    const area = document.getElementById('da-area-' + id)?.value || '';
    const meta = document.getElementById('da-meta-' + id);
    if (!meta) return;
    let parts = [];
    if (hazard) parts.push(hazard.replace(' — ', ' '));
    if (area) parts.push(area + ' sq ft');
    meta.textContent = parts.join('  |  ');
  }
  function removeDesignArea(id) {
    const card = document.getElementById('design-area-' + id);
    if (card) {
      card.style.opacity = '0';
      card.style.transform = 'translateX(-8px)';
      card.style.transition = 'all 0.2s ease';
      setTimeout(() => {
        card.remove();
        // Show empty state if no areas remain
        const list = document.getElementById('design-area-list');
        if (list && list.children.length === 0) showDesignAreaEmpty();
      }, 200);
    }
  }
  function showDesignAreaEmpty() {
    const list = document.getElementById('design-area-list');
    if (!list) return;
    list.innerHTML = `<div class="design-area-empty">
      <div class="design-area-empty-icon">💧</div>
      No design areas added yet. Click <strong>+ Add Design Area</strong> above to begin.
    </div>`;
  }
  // Initialize empty state on load
  function initDesignAreas() {
    const list = document.getElementById('design-area-list');
    if (list) showDesignAreaEmpty();
  }
  // ── SUPPLEMENTS ──
  const SUPPLEMENTS = {
    restaurant:   { label: 'Restaurant / Food Service', icon: '🍳', section: 'supp-restaurant' },
    woodworking:  { label: 'Woodworking / Lumber',      icon: '🪚', section: 'supp-woodworking' },
    warehouse:    { label: 'Warehouse / Distribution',  icon: '🏭', section: 'supp-warehouse' },
    autoservice:  { label: 'Auto Service / Repair',     icon: '🔧', section: 'supp-autoservice' },
    sprinkler:    { label: 'Sprinkler — Detailed',      icon: '💧', section: 'supp-sprinkler' },
    apartments:   { label: 'Apartments / Condominiums', icon: '🏢', section: 'supp-apartments' },
    addbuilding:  { label: 'Additional Buildings',      icon: '🏗️', section: 'supp-addbuilding' },
  };
  // ── GL MODULES ──
  const GL_MODULES = {
    premises: { label: 'Premises Liability', icon: '🏛️', section: 'gl-premises' },
    products: { label: 'Products Liability', icon: '📦', section: 'gl-products' },
    fleet:    { label: 'Small Fleet',        icon: '🚛', section: 'gl-fleet' },
  };
  const activeGL = new Set();
  function toggleGL(id) {
    const card = document.getElementById('gl-card-' + id);
    const label = card.querySelector('.supp-toggle-label');
    const isActive = activeGL.has(id);
    if (isActive) {
      activeGL.delete(id);
      card.classList.remove('active-supp');
      label.textContent = 'Inactive';
      removeGLNav(id);
    } else {
      activeGL.add(id);
      card.classList.add('active-supp');
      label.textContent = 'Active';
      addGLNav(id);
    }
  }
  function addGLNav(id) {
    const container = document.getElementById('gl-nav-items');
    if (document.getElementById('gl-nav-' + id)) return;
    const m = GL_MODULES[id];
    const div = document.createElement('div');
    div.className = 'supp-nav-item';
    div.id = 'gl-nav-' + id;
    div.setAttribute('data-section', m.section);
    div.onclick = function() { showSection(m.section, this); };
    div.innerHTML = '<div class="supp-dot"></div> ' + m.icon + ' ' + m.label + '<span class="supp-badge">GL</span>';
    container.appendChild(div);
  }
  function removeGLNav(id) {
    const el = document.getElementById('gl-nav-' + id);
    if (el) el.remove();
    const active = document.querySelector('.section-panel.active');
    if (active && active.id === 'section-' + GL_MODULES[id].section) {
      showSection('gl-manager', document.querySelector('[data-section="gl-manager"]'));
    }
  }
  // Occupancy → supplement mapping for auto-suggest
  const OCCUPANCY_MAP = {
    'Restaurant / Food Service':  ['restaurant'],
    'Woodworking / Lumber':       ['woodworking'],
    'Warehouse / Distribution':   ['warehouse'],
    'Auto Service / Repair':      ['autoservice'],
    'Apartments / Condominiums':  ['apartments'],
  };
  const activeSupplements = new Set();
  const suggestedSupplements = new Set();
  function handleOccupancyChange(val) {
    // Clear previous suggestions
    suggestedSupplements.forEach(id => {
      const badge = document.getElementById('supp-card-' + id)?.querySelector('.auto-suggested');
      if (badge) badge.remove();
    });
    suggestedSupplements.clear();
    const matches = OCCUPANCY_MAP[val] || [];
    matches.forEach(id => {
      suggestedSupplements.add(id);
      const card = document.getElementById('supp-card-' + id);
      if (card && !card.querySelector('.auto-suggested')) {
        const badge = document.createElement('div');
        badge.className = 'auto-suggested';
        badge.textContent = 'AUTO-SUGGESTED';
        card.appendChild(badge);
      }
      // Auto-activate if not already active
      if (!activeSupplements.has(id)) {
        toggleSupplement(id);
      }
    });
    if (matches.length > 0) {
      // Show a non-blocking notice instead of alert
      showSuppToast(matches.map(id => SUPPLEMENTS[id].label).join(', '));
    }
  }
  function showSuppToast(names) {
    let toast = document.getElementById('supp-toast');
    if (!toast) {
      toast = document.createElement('div');
      toast.id = 'supp-toast';
      toast.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;bottom:80px;left:50%;transform:translateX(-50%);background:#0d1b2a;color:#e2c97e;padding:10px 20px;border-radius:8px;font-size:13px;font-family:IBM Plex Sans,sans-serif;z-index:999;box-shadow:0 4px 20px rgba(0,0,0,0.3);border:1px solid #c9a84c;transition:opacity 0.4s;';
      document.body.appendChild(toast);
    }
    toast.textContent = '✓ Supplement auto-activated: ' + names;
    toast.style.opacity = '1';
    setTimeout(() => { toast.style.opacity = '0'; }, 3500);
  }
  function toggleSupplement(id) {
    const card = document.getElementById('supp-card-' + id);
    const label = card.querySelector('.supp-toggle-label');
    const isActive = activeSupplements.has(id);
    if (isActive) {
      activeSupplements.delete(id);
      card.classList.remove('active-supp');
      label.textContent = 'Inactive';
      removeSuppNav(id);
    } else {
      activeSupplements.add(id);
      card.classList.add('active-supp');
      label.textContent = 'Active';
      addSuppNav(id);
    }
    updateProgress();
  }
  function addSuppNav(id) {
    const container = document.getElementById('supp-nav-items');
    if (document.getElementById('supp-nav-' + id)) return;
    const s = SUPPLEMENTS[id];
    const div = document.createElement('div');
    div.className = 'supp-nav-item';
    div.id = 'supp-nav-' + id;
    div.setAttribute('data-section', s.section);
    div.onclick = function() { showSection(s.section, this); };
    div.innerHTML = '<div class="supp-dot"></div> ' + s.icon + ' ' + s.label + '<span class="supp-badge">SUPP</span>';
    container.appendChild(div);
  }
  function removeSuppNav(id) {
    const el = document.getElementById('supp-nav-' + id);
    if (el) el.remove();
    // If currently viewing this supplement, go back to manager
    const active = document.querySelector('.section-panel.active');
    if (active && active.id === 'section-' + SUPPLEMENTS[id].section) {
      showSection('supp-manager', document.querySelector('[data-section="supp-manager"]'));
    }
  }

              <option>Communicating</option>
            </select>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="divider"></div>
      <!-- C — Construction -->
      <div style="padding:0 16px;">
        <div style="font-size:10px;font-weight:600;color:var(--navy);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.08em;margin-bottom:10px;padding-top:12px;">C — Construction</div>
        <div class="form-grid">
          <div class="field">
            <label>Year Built</label>
            <input type="number" id="${b}-year-built" placeholder="e.g. 1998">
          </div>
          <div class="field">
            <label>Total Square Footage</label>
            <input type="number" id="${b}-sq-footage" placeholder="sq ft">
          </div>
          <div class="field">
            <label>Number of Storeys</label>
            <input type="number" id="${b}-storeys" placeholder="e.g. 1">
          </div>
          <div class="field">
            <label>ISO Construction Class</label>
            <select id="${b}-construction-class">
              <option value="">— Select —</option>
              <option>Class 1 — Frame</option>

  function addBuilding() {
    buildingCount++;
    const container = document.getElementById('additional-buildings-container');
    const div = document.createElement('div');
    div.id = `building-wrapper-${buildingCount}`;
    div.innerHTML = buildingCOPEHTML(buildingCount);
    container.appendChild(div);
    // Scroll to new building
    div.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
    showToast(`✓ Building ${buildingCount} added`);
  }
  function removeBuilding(num) {
    if (!confirm(`Remove Building ${num} and all its data?`)) return;
    const el = document.getElementById(`building-wrapper-${num}`);
    if (el) el.remove();
    showToast(`Building ${num} removed`);
  }
    // ── PUBLISH / UNPUBLISH REPORT ──
  async function togglePublishReport(id, isPublished, inspectionId, insuredName) {
    const action = isPublished ? 'unpublish' : 'publish';
    const msg = isPublished
      ? `Unpublish report for ${insuredName || inspectionId}? The client link will stop working.`
      : `Publish report for ${insuredName || inspectionId}? The client will be able to view it online using their reference number.`;
    if (!confirm(msg)) return;
    try {
      const { error } = await _supabase
        .from('inspections')
        .update({ report_published: !isPublished })
        .eq('id', id);
      if (error) throw error;
      if (!isPublished) {
        // Show the client link
        const link = `${window.location.origin}/report?ref=${inspectionId}`;
        showToast('✓ Report published — client link ready');
        // Show copyable link in a small prompt
        setTimeout(() => {
          if (confirm('Report published! Click OK to copy the client link to clipboard.')) {
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(link).then(() => showToast('✓ Link copied to clipboard'));
          }
        }, 400);
      } else {
        showToast('✓ Report unpublished — client link deactivated');
      }
      loadDashboard();
    } catch(e) {
      showToast('⚠ Failed to update: ' + (e.message || e), 'warn');
    }
  }
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  // PORTAL SETTINGS — Access Code Management
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  async function showPortalSettings() {
    const wrap = document.getElementById('portal-settings-wrap');
    wrap.style.display = 'block';
    wrap.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
    // Load current code from Supabase settings table
    const input = document.getElementById('portal-access-code-input');
    input.value = 'Loading...';
    input.disabled = true;
    try {
      const { data, error } = await _supabase
        .from('platform_settings')
        .select('value')
        .eq('key', 'portal_access_code')
        .single();
      input.disabled = false;
      if (error || !data) {
        // No code set yet — show the default
        input.value = 'Sanket2026';
      } else {
        input.value = data.value;
      }
    } catch(e) {
      input.disabled = false;
      input.value = 'Sanket2026';
      console.warn('Could not load access code:', e.message);
    }
  }
  async function saveAccessCode() {
    const input = document.getElementById('portal-access-code-input');
    const msg   = document.getElementById('access-code-msg');
    const newCode = input.value.trim();
    if (!newCode) {
      msg.textContent = '⚠ Please enter a code before saving.';
      msg.style.color = '#e53e3e';
      msg.style.display = 'block';
      return;
    }
    msg.textContent = '⏳ Saving...';
    msg.style.color = 'var(--slate)';
    msg.style.display = 'block';
    try {
      // Upsert — insert if not exists, update if it does
      const { error } = await _supabase
        .from('platform_settings')
        .upsert({ key: 'portal_access_code', value: newCode }, { onConflict: 'key' });
      if (error) throw error;
      msg.textContent = '✓ Access code updated successfully. New code is live immediately.';
      msg.style.color = '#276749';
      showToast('✓ Portal access code updated to: ' + newCode);
    } catch(e) {
      msg.textContent = '⚠ Failed to save: ' + (e.message || 'Please try again.');
      msg.style.color = '#e53e3e';
      console.error(e);
    }
  }
    // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  // SPRINKLER GRADE CALCULATOR
  // Based on SRC methodology + NFPA 25 deficiency scoring
  // Starting score = 100, demerits reduce score, score maps to Grade 1-5
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  function calculateSprinklerGrade() {
    const demeritFields = [
      'spk-hazard-class', 'spk-design-match', 'spk-qod',
      'spk-content-comb', 'spk-ceiling', 'spk-obstruction',
      'spk-openings', 'spk-internal-exp',
      'spk-water-adequacy', 'spk-connections', 'spk-valve-access',
      'spk-drain-drop', 'spk-head-condition', 'spk-piping',
      'spk-riser-heat', 'spk-fdc', 'spk-monitoring',
      'spk-annual-insp', 'spk-pump-test', 'spk-trip-test',
      'spk-5yr-insp', 'spk-underground-test', 'spk-impairments'
    ];
    // Check all fields have been completed
    var incomplete = [];
    var fieldLabels = {
      'spk-hazard-class':'Occupancy Hazard Classification',
      'spk-design-match':'System Design vs. Occupancy',
      'spk-qod':'Dry Pipe QOD Trip Time',
      'spk-content-comb':'Combustibility of Contents',
      'spk-ceiling':'High Ceiling / Storage Clearance',
      'spk-obstruction':'Sprinkler Obstruction',
      'spk-openings':'Unprotected Vertical Openings',
      'spk-internal-exp':'Internal Exposure',
      'spk-water-adequacy':'Water Supply Adequacy',
      'spk-connections':'Water Supply Connections',
      'spk-valve-access':'Control Valve Accessibility',
      'spk-drain-drop':'Pressure Drop on 2" Drain Test',
      'spk-head-condition':'Sprinkler Head Condition',
      'spk-piping':'Piping Condition',
      'spk-riser-heat':'Riser Room Heating',
      'spk-fdc':'Fire Department Connection',
      'spk-monitoring':'Central Station Monitoring',
      'spk-annual-insp':'Annual Inspection Currency',
      'spk-pump-test':'Fire Pump Annual Test',
      'spk-trip-test':'Dry Pipe / Deluge Valve Trip Test',
      'spk-5yr-insp':'5-Year Internal Obstruction Inspection',
      'spk-underground-test':'Underground Acceptance Testing',
      'spk-impairments':'Open Impairments'
    };
    demeritFields.forEach(id => {
      const el = document.getElementById(id);
      if (el && el.value === '') incomplete.push(fieldLabels[id] || id);
    });
    if (incomplete.length > 0) {
      showToast('⚠ Please complete all fields before calculating: ' + incomplete.slice(0,3).join(', ') + (incomplete.length > 3 ? ' + ' + (incomplete.length-3) + ' more' : ''), 'warn');
      return;
    }
    let totalDemerits = 0;
    demeritFields.forEach(id => {
      const el = document.getElementById(id);
      if (el && el.value !== '' && !isNaN(parseInt(el.value))) {
        totalDemerits += parseInt(el.value);
      }
    });
    // Cap demerits at 100
    totalDemerits = Math.min(totalDemerits, 100);
    const score = Math.max(0, 100 - totalDemerits);
    // Map score to grade
    let grade, gradeDesc, gradeColor;
    if (score >= 90) {
      grade = 1;
      gradeDesc = 'Grade 1 — Fully Effective: Water supply adequate, design matches occupancy, NFPA 25 current, ULC monitored. Maximum sprinkler credit applicable.';
      gradeColor = '#276749';
    } else if (score >= 75) {
      grade = 2;
      gradeDesc = 'Grade 2 — Effective with Minor Deficiencies: One or two non-critical items outstanding. Full sprinkler credit with recommendations noted.';
      gradeColor = '#7B5E00';
    } else if (score >= 55) {
      grade = 3;
      gradeDesc = 'Grade 3 — Partially Effective: Moderate deficiencies in design, coverage, or maintenance. Reduced credit — 30/90-day recommendations required.';
      gradeColor = '#C05621';
    } else if (score >= 35) {
      grade = 4;
      gradeDesc = 'Grade 4 — Marginally Effective: Significant deficiencies across multiple areas. Minimal credit — Immediate recommendations, refer to underwriter.';
      gradeColor = '#C53030';
    } else {
      grade = 5;
      gradeDesc = 'Grade 5 — Ineffective / Compromised: System impaired, water critically inadequate, or severely underdesigned for hazard. No sprinkler credit — treat as unprotected.';
      gradeColor = '#C53030';
    }
    // Update display
    document.getElementById('spk-demerit-total').textContent = totalDemerits;
    document.getElementById('spk-score').textContent = score;
    const gradeDisplay = document.getElementById('spk-grade-display');
    gradeDisplay.textContent = 'Grade ' + grade;
    gradeDisplay.style.color = gradeColor;
    document.getElementById('spk-grade-desc').textContent = gradeDesc;
    // Auto-set the final grade dropdown
    const finalSel = document.getElementById('spk-final-grade');
    if (finalSel) finalSel.value = String(grade);
    showToast('✓ Sprinkler Grade calculated: Grade ' + grade + ' (Score: ' + score + '/100)');
  }
    // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  // RECOMMENDATIONS LIBRARY — Supabase search & insert
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  let recLibraryData = [];      // cached from Supabase
  let recLibraryLoaded = false;
  async function openRecLibrary() {
    document.getElementById('rec-library-overlay').classList.add('open');
    document.getElementById('rec-lib-search').focus();
    if (!recLibraryLoaded) {
      await loadRecLibrary();
    } else {
      filterRecLibrary();
    }
  }
  function closeRecLibrary(e) {
    if (e && e.target !== document.getElementById('rec-library-overlay')) return;
    document.getElementById('rec-library-overlay').classList.remove('open');
  }
  async function loadRecLibrary() {
    const resultsEl = document.getElementById('rec-lib-results');
    resultsEl.innerHTML = '<div class="rec-lib-empty">⏳ Loading recommendations from database...</div>';
    try {
      const { data, error } = await _supabase
        .from('recommendations')
        .select('rec_id, category, subcategory, priority, responsible_party, title, rec_text')
        .eq('active', true)
        .order('category')
        .order('priority');
      if (error) {
        console.error('Supabase error:', JSON.stringify(error));
        throw error;
      }
      recLibraryData = data || [];
      recLibraryLoaded = true;
      console.log('Loaded ' + recLibraryData.length + ' recommendations');
      filterRecLibrary();
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Rec library load error:', err.message || err);
      resultsEl.innerHTML = '<div class="rec-lib-empty">⚠️ ' + (err.message || 'Could not load recommendations library. Check your connection and try again.') + '</div>';
    }
  }
  function filterRecLibrary() {
    const query    = (document.getElementById('rec-lib-search').value || '').toLowerCase().trim();
    const catFilter  = document.getElementById('rec-lib-cat').value;
    const prioFilter = document.getElementById('rec-lib-prio').value;
    const resultsEl  = document.getElementById('rec-lib-results');
    const countEl    = document.getElementById('rec-lib-count');
    let filtered = recLibraryData;
    if (catFilter)  filtered = filtered.filter(r => r.category === catFilter);
    if (prioFilter) filtered = filtered.filter(r => r.priority === prioFilter);
    if (query) {
      filtered = filtered.filter(r =>
        (r.title    || '').toLowerCase().includes(query) ||
        (r.rec_text || '').toLowerCase().includes(query) ||
        (r.category || '').toLowerCase().includes(query) ||
        (r.subcategory || '').toLowerCase().includes(query)
      );
    }
    // Default: show all if no filters set
    if (!query && !catFilter && !prioFilter) {
      filtered = recLibraryData;
    }
    countEl.textContent = filtered.length + ' of ' + recLibraryData.length + ' recommendations';
    if (filtered.length === 0) {
      resultsEl.innerHTML = '<div class="rec-lib-empty">No recommendations match your search. Try a different keyword or clear the filters.</div>';
      return;
    }
    resultsEl.innerHTML = filtered.map(function(r) {
      var prioClass = (r.priority || '').replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9-]/g,'');
      var preview   = (r.rec_text || '').substring(0, 200);
      if (r.rec_text && r.rec_text.length > 200) preview += '...';
      var safeTitle = (r.title    || '').replace(/"/g, '&quot;').replace(/'/g, '&#39;');
      var safeText  = (r.rec_text || '').replace(/"/g, '&quot;').replace(/'/g, '&#39;');
      var safePrio  = (r.priority  || '').replace(/"/g, '&quot;').replace(/'/g, '&#39;');
      var safeCat   = (r.category  || '').replace(/"/g, '&quot;').replace(/'/g, '&#39;');
      return '<div class="rec-lib-item prio-' + prioClass + '">' +
        '<div class="rec-lib-item-header">' +
          '<span class="rec-lib-badge badge-' + prioClass + '">' + (r.priority || '') + '</span>' +
          '<span class="rec-lib-title">' + (r.title || '') + '</span>' +
          '<span class="rec-lib-cat">' + (r.subcategory || r.category || '') + '</span>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div class="rec-lib-preview">' + preview + '</div>' +
        '<button class="rec-lib-insert-btn" ' +
          'onclick=\'insertRecFromLibrary(this)\' ' +
          'data-title="' + safeTitle + '" ' +
          'data-text="'  + safeText  + '" ' +
          'data-prio="'  + safePrio  + '" ' +
          'data-cat="'   + safeCat   + '">' +
          '&#xff0b; Insert' +
        '</button>' +
        '<div style="clear:both"></div>' +
      '</div>';
    }).join('');
  }
  function insertRecFromLibrary(btn) {
    var title    = (btn.getAttribute('data-title') || '').replace(/&quot;/g,'"').replace(/&#39;/g,"'");
    var text     = (btn.getAttribute('data-text')  || '').replace(/&quot;/g,'"').replace(/&#39;/g,"'");
    var priority = btn.getAttribute('data-prio')  || '';
    var category = btn.getAttribute('data-cat')   || '';
    var prioMap = { 'Immediate': 'high', '30-Day': 'high', '90-Day': 'med', 'Advisory': 'low' };
    var level = prioMap[priority] || 'med';
    // If rec-1 textarea is empty, populate it instead of creating rec-2
    var rec1 = document.getElementById('rec-1');
    if (rec1) {
      var rec1ta = rec1.querySelector('textarea');
      if (rec1ta && !rec1ta.value.trim()) {
        rec1ta.value = text;
        // Pre-fill title field with library rec title
        var rec1title = rec1.querySelector('.rec-title-field');
        if (rec1title && title) rec1title.value = title;
        // Set priority
        rec1.className = 'rec-item priority-' + level;
        var priorityLbl = rec1.querySelector('[data-level="' + level + '"]');
        if (priorityLbl) setRecPriority(priorityLbl, 'rec-1', level);
        // Add delete button if not already there
        addDeleteBtn(rec1);
        document.getElementById('rec-library-overlay').classList.remove('open');
        showToast('Recommendation inserted into #1: ' + title.substring(0, 50));
        setTimeout(function() { rec1.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' }); }, 200);
        return;
      }
    }
    recCount++;
    var div = document.createElement('div');
    div.className = 'rec-item priority-' + level;
    div.id = 'rec-' + recCount;
    var catToSection = {
      'Fire Protection': 'Protection — Fire',
      'Electrical': 'Construction',
      'Life Safety': 'Protection — Fire',
      'Premises Liability': 'Other',
      'Housekeeping': 'Housekeeping',
      'Safety & Compliance': 'Safety / Compliance',
      'Security': 'Protection — Security',
      'Spray Finishing': 'Occupancy',
      'Heating Systems': 'Construction',
      'Flammable & Combustible Liquids': 'Occupancy',
      'Structural & Water Damage': 'Construction',
      'Warehouse & Storage': 'Occupancy',
      'Woodworking Operations': 'Occupancy',
      'Auto Service': 'Occupancy',
      'Fleet Safety': 'Other',
      'Building Systems': 'Construction',
      'Pool, Playground & Amenities': 'Other',
      'Multi-Residential': 'Occupancy',
      'Contractors & Administration': 'Other'
    };
    var sectionVal = catToSection[category] || 'Other';
    var sectionOptions = ['Construction','Occupancy','Protection — Fire','Protection — Security','Exposure','Safety / Compliance','Housekeeping','Other'];
    var sectionOpts = sectionOptions.map(function(o) {
      return '<option' + (o === sectionVal ? ' selected' : '') + '>' + o + '</option>';
    }).join('');
    var hHigh = level === 'high' ? ' selected' : '';
    var hMed  = level === 'med'  ? ' selected' : '';
    var hLow  = level === 'low'  ? ' selected' : '';
    var rc = recCount;
    div.innerHTML =
      '<div class="rec-header">' +
        '<span class="rec-num">#' + rc + '</span>' +
        '<div class="radio-group" style="flex-wrap:nowrap;gap:6px">' +
